259	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE AGRICULTURAL CENSUS ACT, 1958 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE AGRICULTURAL CENSUS ACT, 1958 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ACT NO. XLI OF 1958).[23rd September, 1958]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 An Act to provide for certain matters for the purpose of taking agricultural census.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS in a general meeting of the Food and Agricultural Organization of the United Nations a decision has been taken urging the member countries to take agricultural census;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS it is expedient to take agricultural census in pursuance of the said decision and to provide for certain matters for that purpose;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS in pursuance of the proviso to Article 108 of the Constitution the Governors of the Provinces of East Pakistan and West  Pakistan have been consulted;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the Agricultural Census Act, 1958.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 2[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force on such date as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) “census” means agricultural census;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “census officer” means an officer appointed for the purpose of carrying out the provisions of this Act 3[ ;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “Director-General” means the Director-General of the Bangladesh Bureau of Statistics.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Census officers</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. 4[ (1) The Director-General may-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        make plan and supervise the taking of census throughout Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        appoint census officers to take, aid in or supervise the taking of, the census within any specified area.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) [Omitted by section 5 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) A declaration in writing, signed by any authority authorised by the 5[ Director-General] in this behalf, that a person has been duly appointed a census officer shall be conclusive proof of such appointment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Collection of information for census</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) For the purpose of taking census, information shall be collected on or with respect to the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        land ownership and land tenure;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        land unit and subdivision of land;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        land utilisation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        crop acreage and production;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        livestock and poultry;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         employment in agriculture;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        agricultural population;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h)        agricultural power and machinery;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) irrigation and drainage;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j) fertilisers and soil dressing;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(k)        wood and fishery products;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(l) agricultural credit;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(m)       agriculture and sericulture;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(n) fruit and vegetable products; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(o) such other matters as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, specify.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) For the purpose of collecting information referred to in sub-section (1), the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, prepare such questionnaire as it thinks fit and a census officer may require any person within his jurisdiction to give answers to such questionnaire and to such other questions relevant to the questionnaire as he may think fit to ask.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Any person who is required to give answers to the questionnaire and other relevant questions under sub-section (2) shall be legally bound to give answers to the best of his knowledge or belief.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Crop-cutting experiment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) For the purpose of collecting information referred to in sub-section (1) of section 4, crop-cutting experiments may be conducted, and for such experiments any land in any area may be selected.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The owners or occupiers of lands or their agents or servants shall allow such access to the census officers and other persons assisting them to their lands as may be necessary for the conduct of crop-cutting experiments.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The owner or other person entitled to the crop shall be paid such compensation for any loss or damage caused to him by the conduct of crop-cutting experiments as the Government may prescribe.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Access to census officers to premises and lands</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. Every person owning or occupying any house, premises or lands shall allow the census officers such access thereto as they may require for the purposes of the census and shall allow them to paint on, affix to, or dig in, the house, premises or lands such letters, mark or objects as may be necessary for the said purpose.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalties</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. (a) Any census officer or any person lawfully required to give assistance towards the taking of a census who refuses or neglects to use reasonable diligence in performing any duty imposed upon him or in obeying any order issued to him in accordance with this Act or any rule made thereunder, or any person who hinders or obstructs another person in performing any such duty or in obeying any such order, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        any census officer who knowingly makes any false return or, without the previous sanction of the 6[ Government], discloses any information which he has received by means of, or for the purposes of, a census return, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        any person who intentionally gives a false answer to, or refuses to answer to the best of his knowledge or belief, to the questionnaire or other relevant question asked of him by a census officer which he is legally bound to answer, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        any person occupying any house, premises or land who refuses to allow a census officer such reasonable access thereto as he is required under section 6 to allow, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        any person who removes, obliterates, alters or damages without proper authority or before the completion of the census any letters, marks or objects which have been painted, affixed or dug for the purposes of the census, shall be punishable with fine which may extend to five hundred 7[ taka].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Sanction for prosecution under this Act</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. No prosecution under this Act shall be instituted except with the previous sanction of the 8[ Government] or of an authority authorised in this behalf by the 9[ Government].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Prosecution under other laws</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. Nothing in this Act shall be deemed to prevent any person from being prosecuted under any other law for any act or omission under this Act which constitutes an offence under such other law:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that no such prosecution shall be instituted except with the previous sanction referred to in section 8.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Jurisdiction</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. No court inferior to that of a Magistrate of the second class shall try an offence under this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Census records not open to inspection</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. No person shall have a right to inspect any book, register or record made by a census officer in the discharge of his duties as such, and notwithstanding anything to the contrary in the Evidence Act, 1872, no entry in any such book, register or record shall be admissible as evidence in any civil proceeding whatsoever, or in any criminal proceedings, other than a prosecution under this Act or under any other law for any act or omission under this Act which constitutes an offence under such other law.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Preparation of statistical abstracts</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. The 10[ Director-General] or such person as the Government may authorise in this behalf may, if he thinks fit, at the request and cost (to be determined by him) of any local authority or person, cause abstracts to be prepared and supplied containing any such statistical information as can be derived from the census returns being information which is not contained in any published report and which, in his opinion, it is reasonable for that authority or person to require.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Census officers to be public servants</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. All census officers shall be deemed to be public servants within the meaning of section 21 of the 11[ * * *] Penal Code.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, unless otherwise provided, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government” by section 2 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the word “Pakistan” by section 3 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The semi-colon (;) was substituted for the full-stop (.) and clause (c) was added by section 4 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 Sub-section (1) was substituted by section 5 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The word “Director-General” was substituted for the words “Central Government” by section 5 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government or the Provincial Government” by section 6 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The word “taka” was substituted for the word “rupees” by section 6 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 7 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 7 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The word “Director-General” was substituted for the words and comma “Census Commissioner or any Joint Census Commissioner, Deputy Census Commissioner or Assistant Census Commissioner” by section 8 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">11 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by section 9 of the Agricultural Census (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XXII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
260	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">   THE ANIMALS SLAUGHTER (RESTRICTION) AND MEAT CONTROL ACT, 1957 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE ANIMALS SLAUGHTER (RESTRICTION) AND MEAT CONTROL ACT, 1957 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ACT NO. VIII OF 1957).[23rd April, 1957]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An  Act to provide for restriction on the slaughter of certain animals and for control of consumption of meat thereof. 1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is necessary to provide for powers to restrict the slaughter of animals and to control the consumption of meat thereof;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the 2[ * * *] Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control Act, 1957.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 3[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “animal” means any bull, bullock, cow, ox, heifer, 4[ calf, buffalo, goat and sheep];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “carcase” means the dead body or any portion of the dead body of an animal as defined in clause (a);</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “catering establishment” means any hotel, restaurant, eating house, cafe, canteen, and includes any other place of a like nature open to the public or to any limited class of the public where meat in any form is consumed or procurable;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “meat” means the flesh or other edible portion of any animal which has been slaughtered in a slaughter-house as defined in clause (f) ;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “prohibited day” means a day on which the slaughter of animal and the sale of meat thereof is prohibited by the Government by notification in the official Gazette; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         “slaughter-house” means any place used for the slaughter of any animal for the purpose of selling the flesh thereof as meat or otherwise, but excludes any slaughter-house belonging to or maintained by the 5[ Armed Forces of Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">No slaughter of animal or sale of flesh or meat on prohibited day</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) No person shall, during the period of 24 hours commencing at sunset on the day immediately preceding the prohibited day, slaughter any animal at any slaughter-house or at any other place for the sale of its meat.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No person shall on any prohibited day sell or expose for sale any meat at any market or other place.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Restriction on supply and sale in the catering establishment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. No owner, Manager or person in charge of or having control of any catering establishment shall on a prohibited day sell or expose for sale or serve, supply or cause to be served, supplied or sold any food containing meat in such catering establishment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Restrictions on slaughter of animals</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. No person shall slaughter or cause or permit to be slaughtered or offer for slaughter in a slaughter-house-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ (a) a she-goat or ewe below the age of two years or any other female animal below the age of three years;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        a he-goat, ram or lamb of or below the age of one year or any other male animal of or below the age of seven years, if such animal is used or is capable of being used for draught or breeding purposes;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        a she-goat or ewe of or below the age of five years or any other female animal of or below the age of ten years, if such animal is not unsuitable for bearing offspring and is capable of producing milk; or]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        any female animal which is pregnant or is in milk:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that nothing in this section shall apply to any animal which on account of any bodily injury, illness or other infirmity is certified in writing by an officer of the 7[ Directorate of Livestock Services not below the rank of Thana Livestock Officer],-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         in the case of an animal falling under clause (a), to be unlikely to live or to be fit for any of the purposes enumerated in clauses (b) or (c) as the case may be;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        in the case of an animal falling under clauses (b) or (c), to be unfit for the purposes respectively enumerated therein; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       in the case of an animal falling under clause (d), to be unfit to be allowed to remain pregnant or produce milk:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided further that if any such certificate is proved to have been procured through fraud or collusion it will be treated as invalid and the officer giving such certificate shall be severely dealt with.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power of authorised Officer</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) Any Officer authorised by Government by notification in the official Gazette in this behalf may-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        at any time enter and inspect any place used or believed to be used for the slaughter of animals for the purpose of selling or consuming the meat thereof or any place where meat is sold or exposed for sale or where any food containing meat is served, supplied or sold if there is reason to believe that meat has been or is being served, supplied, sold or exposed for sale in such place in contravention of the provisions of this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        seize any animal or the carcase thereof found in such place, or any meat, receptacle, covering in which such meat is found or any other article by means of which he has reason to believe that contravention of any provision of the Act has been or is being or is likely to be committed;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        require the owner, Manager or person in charge or control of any slaughter-house or of any catering establishment to furnish such information as may be necessary for the purpose of securing compliance with this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Officer taking action under sub-section (1) of this section shall immediately report the matter to the nearest Magistrate having jurisdiction to enquire into or try the case or to the Officer-in-charge of the nearest police-station who on receiving such report shall have the same powers of investigation as he may exercise in a cognizable case, but shall not arrest without warrant:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Officer-in-charge or any other officer exercising any power under this Act shall have the power to dispose of any carcase by sale or otherwise as may appear to him to be most suitable if he is satisfied that the carcase is liable to speedy decay.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The report of the officer-in-charge mentioned in sub-section (2), submitted to the Magistrate shall be deemed to be a report under clause (b) of sub-section (1) of section 190 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalty</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. If any person contravenes any provisions of this Act,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        he shall on conviction by a competent Court be punishable with imprisonment of either description for a term which may extend to 6 months or with fine not exceeding 8[ Taka 1000] or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        without prejudice to the punishment referred to in clause (a), any Court trying the offence may order that any animal or the carcase of such animal in respect of which the Court is satisfied that the offence has been committed, shall be forfeited to the Government and disposed of by sale or otherwise as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Deposit of sums</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. All sums realised under sub-section (2) of section 6 or under section 7 shall be deposited in the Government Treasury in such manner as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Exceptions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. 9[ (1) Nothing in this Act shall apply to animals slaughtered or to be slaughtered-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        on the day of Id-uz-Zoha and Id-ul-Fitre and the two days succeeding each of those festivals, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        for preparation of goat tissue vaccine or for any other research work in the vaccine and research laboratories of the Directorate of Livestock Services.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Government may from time to time prescribe such other occasions in relation to which any or all of the provisions of this Act shall not apply.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10.       The Government may make rules to give effect to the provisions of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Public servant</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11.       Any person empowered to perform any function under this Act shall be deemed to be a public servant within the meaning of section 21 of the 10[ * * *] Penal Code.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Indemnity</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12.        (1) No Civil or Criminal proceeding shall lie against any person for anything done or intended to be done in good faith under this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No proceeding shall lie against the Government for any action taken under this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[Repealed]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13.       [Repeal and saving.- Repealed by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the East Pakistan Repealing and Amending Ordinance, 1966 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. XIII of 1966).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 2 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by section 3 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words “Bangladesh” were substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by section 3 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The words and commas “calf, buffalo, goat and sheep” were substituted for the words “calf and buffalo” by section 4 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “Armed Forces of Bangladesh” were substituted for the words “Pakistan State Forces” by section 4 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 Clauses (a), (b) and (c) were substituted by section 5 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The words “Directorate of Livestock Services not below the rank of Thana Livestock Officer” were substituted for the words “East Pakistan Directorate of Animal Husbandry not below the rank of Assistant Animal Husbandry Officer” by section 5 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The word and figure “Taka 1000” were substituted for the letters and figure “Rs. 200” by section 6 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 Sub-section (1) was substituted by section 7 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by section 8 of the Animals Slaughter (Restriction) and Meat Control (Amendment) Ordinance, 1983 (Ordinance No. XVIII of 1983)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
261	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE BANGLADESH SMALL AND COTTAGE INDUSTRIES CORPORATION ACT, 1957 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE </strong><strong>BANGLADESH</strong><strong> SMALL AND COTTAGE INDUSTRIES CORPORATION ACT, 1957 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ACT NO. XVII OF 1957).[21st May, 1957]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 An Act to establish a Corporation for the purpose of promoting the development of 2[ small and cottage industries in Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to establish a Corporation for the purpose of promoting the development of 3[ small and cottage industries in Bangladesh];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. 4[ (1) This Act may be called the Bangladesh Small and Cottage Industries Corporation Act, 1957.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 5[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force on such date as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Interpretation </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “Board” means the Board of Directors of the Corporation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “borrower” means any person or persons or body of persons, whether incorporated or not, to whom a loan is made by the Corporation under this Act and the successors and assignees of such person or persons;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ (bb) ‘Chairman' means the Chairman of the Board;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “Corporation” means the Small and Cottage Industries Corporation established by this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ (cc) “cottage industry” means an Industry which is carried on primarily with the help of the members of a family either as a whole time or part time occupation and the total investment of which does not exceed such amount as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, fix but shall not include a factory under the Factories Act, 1965 (E. P. Act IV of 1965);]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9[ (dd) ‘Director' means the Director of the Board;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “prescribed” means prescribed by the rules or regulations made under this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         “scheduled bank” means a bank for the time being included in the list of banks maintained under 10[ clause (1) of Article 37 of the Bangladesh Bank Order, 1972 (P.O. No. 127 of 1972).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">11[ (g) ‘small industry' means an industrial unit which is a factory as defined in clause (f) of section 2 of the Factories Act, 1965 (E.P. Act IV of 1965), and the total investment in fixed assets 12[ excluding] value of land of which does not exceed such amount as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, fix and such notification may be given retrospective effect;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">13[ * * *] and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         “subsidiary corporation” means a corporation sponsored by the Small and Cottage Industries Corporation for the furtherance of its objectives, but operating in a specified area or areas or in respect of one or more specified industry.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Establishment and incorporation of Corporation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) A Corporation to be called “the Small and Cottage Industries Corporation” shall be established as soon as may be after the commencement of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Corporation shall be a body corporate by the name of the Small and Cottage Industries Corporation, having perpetual succession and a common seal, with power, subject to the provisions of this Act, to acquire and hold property, both movable and immovable, and shall by the said name sue and be sued.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Share capital and shareholders</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) The authorised capital of the Corporation shall, in the first instance, be one crore of Taka, divided into one lakh fully paid up shares of 14[ Taka] 100 each. These shares may be issued and allotted by the Corporation from time to time with the previous sanction of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The authorised capital may, with the previous approval of the Government, be increased from time to time by the Corporation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Government shall be a share-holder of the Corporation and shall subscribe to and hold not less than fifty-one per centum of the shares issued by the Corporation at any time; the remaining shares shall be reserved for public subscriptions.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Guarantee by Government</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) The amount subscribed on the shares of the Corporation and a minimum annual dividend thereon shall be guaranteed by the Government. Before the issue of any shares of the Corporation, the Government shall by notification in the official Gazette fix the minimum rates of dividend payable on the shares, and the Corporation shall annually and regularly pay to the share-holders a dividend not less than that fixed by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">If at any time the Corporation is wound up, an amount not less than that subscribed on each share shall be payable to the share-holder.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The shares and debentures of the Corporation shall be deemed to be “approved securities” for purposes of the Trusts Act, 1882.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Management</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) The general direction and administration of the Corporation and its affairs shall vest in a Board of Directors which, may exercise all powers and do all acts and things which may be exercised or done by the Corporation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Board in discharging its functions shall act on commercial considerations and shall be guided on questions of policy by such directions as the Government, which shall be the sole judge whether a question is a question of policy, may give it.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) [Omitted by section 3 of the Bangladesh Small Industries Corporation (Amendment) Act, 1990 (Act No. LVII of 1990).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Composition of Board</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15[ 7. The Board shall consist of seven Directors to be appointed by the Government.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Term of office of Directors</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. Each Director shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) be a whole time officer of the Corporation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        perform such duties as the Board may, by regulations, assign to him;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        divest himself of any directorship or other interest held by him in any other corporation, company, or concern other than public companies sponsored by the Corporation before assuming office as Director;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        subject to the provision of section 11, hold office for a term of three years and may be re-appointed for a further term or terms of such duration as the Government may determine; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        receive such salary and allowances as the Government may determine.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Chairman</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. (1) The Government shall appoint one of the Directors to be the Chairman of the Board, who shall be the chief executive of the Corporation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Subject to his continuing to hold office as a Director, the Chairman shall hold office as Chairman for a term of three years and, subject as aforesaid, shall remain in office as Chairman thereafter until his successor in that office is appointed and may, subject as aforesaid, be appointed to hold that office for a further term or terms as the Government may determine.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) [Omitted by section 7 of the Bangladesh Small Industries Corporation (Amendment) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. XXXIV of 1976).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Finance Director</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. The Government shall appoint one of the Directors to be the Finance Director, who shall exercise such powers and discharge such duties as may be prescribed by rules.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Disqualification of Directors</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. (1) No person shall be or shall continue to be Director who-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        is or at any time has been convicted of an offence involving moral turpitude; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        is or at any time has been adjudicated insolvent; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) is found to be lunatic or becomes of unsound mind; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) is or at any time has been disqualified for employment in, or dismissed from, the service of 16[ the Republic]; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) is a minor.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Government may, by order in writing, remove the Chairman or a Director if he-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) refuses or fails to discharge or becomes, in the opinion of the Government, incapable of discharging his responsibilities under this Act; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        has, in the opinion of the Government, abused his position as Chairman or Director; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        has knowingly acquired or continued to hold, without the permission in writing, of the Government, directly or indirectly, or through a partner, any share or interest in any contract or employment with, by or on behalf of the Corporation, or in any property which, in his knowledge, is likely to benefit or has benefited as a result of the operations of the Corporation; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        has absented himself from three consecutive meetings of the Board without the leave of the Government, in the case of the Chairman, or of the Chairman, in the case of the Director.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Vacancies etc not to invalidate act or proceeding of the Board</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. No act or proceeding or the Board shall be invalid by reason only of the existence of any vacancy in, or any defect in the constitution of, the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appointment of officers, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. (1) Subject to such conditions as may be prescribed by rules, the Corporation may appoint or employ such persons, including consultants and advisers, as it considers necessary for the efficient performance of its functions.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) and (3) [Omitted by section 5 of the Bangladesh Small and Cottage Industries Corporation (Amendment) Act, 1990 (Act No. LVII of 1990).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. [Chairman of the Board.- Omitted by section 11 of the East Pakistan Small Industries Corporation (Second Amendment) Ordinance, 1970 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. XVII of 1970).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Technical Advisory Committee</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15. The Corporation may appoint a Committee of experts to be called “the Technical Advisory Committee” to give it technical advice on schemes submitted to the Corporation for financial assistance or on any point that may be referred to the Committee by the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Restriction on disclosure of information</p><p style="text-align: justify;">16. No information given by a person applying for financial assistance and made known to the Committee shall be disclosed or used by any member of the Committee without the written consent of such person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Meeting of the Board</p><p style="text-align: justify;">17. (1) The meetings of the Board shall be held at such times and at such places as may be prescribed by regulations:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that at least one meeting shall be held in a month:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided further that until such regulations are made in this behalf, such meetings shall be held at such times and at such places as may be determined by the Chairman.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">17[ (2) The number of Directors necessary for a quorum for transacting business at a meeting of the Board shall be three.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Each Director, including the Chairman, shall have one vote but, in the event of an equality of votes, the Chairman shall have a second or casting vote.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The meetings of the Board shall be presided over by the Chairman, and, in his absence, by a Director authorised by him in this behalf, and, in default of such authorisation, by a person elected for the purpose by the Directors present from among themselves.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The minutes of every meeting, stating among other things, the names of the Directors present, shall be drawn up and recorded in a book to be kept for the purpose, and shall be signed by the person presiding at the meeting, and such book shall, at all reasonable times and without charge, be open to inspection of any Director.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">18. [Fees for attending meetings.- Omitted by section 13 of the East Pakistan Small Industries Corporation (Second Amendment) Ordinance, 1970 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. XVII of 1970).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Offices</p><p style="text-align: justify;">19. The Corporation shall establish its Head Office in Dhaka.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Deposit accounts</p><p style="text-align: justify;">20. The Corporation may 18[ * * *] open a deposit account with any approved Schedule Bank.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Investment of funds</p><p style="text-align: justify;">21. The Corporation may invest its funds in such securities or in such other manner as may be prescribed by rules.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Borrowing power</p><p style="text-align: justify;">22. 19[ (1) The Corporation may, with the previous approval of the Government, issue and sell bonds and debentures carrying interest at such rate as may be approved by the Government for the purpose of raising its working capital:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the total of the sums due on such bonds and debentures issued and outstanding and of the contingent liabilities of the Corporation in respect of guarantees or underwriting agreements shall not at any time exceed Taka Twenty-five crore or such higher amount as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, fix.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The bonds and debentures of the Corporation shall be guaranteed by the Government as to the repayment of principal and payment of interest at such rate as may be fixed by the Government at the time when the bonds and debentures are issued.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">20[ (3) The Corporation may, with the prior approval of the Government, borrow money for carrying out the purposes of this Act.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Deposits</p><p style="text-align: justify;">23. The Corporation may accept deposits on such terms and conditions and to such extent as may be approved by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Functions of the Corporation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">24. (1) The 21[ Corporation shall implement industrial policy of the Government in respect of small and cottage industries and] take such measures as it thinks fit to render assistance in the development of 22[ small and cottage industries].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing power, the Corporation may, in order to carry out the purposes of this Act,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) give loans to small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        give loans to subsidiary corporations and commercial and co-operative banks and societies for the development of small and cottage industries:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the loans given or guaranteed under clauses (a) and (b) shall be repayable within a period not exceeding twenty years;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) (i) prepare and submit to the Government schemes for the development of small and cottage industries, including schemes of research and mechanisation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        after these schemes have been approved by the Government, proceed to give effect to them by itself or by sponsoring subsidiary corporations or public companies;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       act as managing agents of such subsidiary corporations or companies, being in any case, represented on their Board of Directors;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       issue the capital required by the aforesaid subsidiary corporations and companies for public subscription;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v)        if any portion of such capital remains unsubscribed for a period of four months from the date of issue, subscribe to such portion;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vi)       underwrite the whole or any portion of the share capital so issued; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vii)      sell or transfer the shares subscribed to under sub-clause (v); provided that no such sale or transfer shall take place at a rate below the market quotation or below the par value of such shares without the previous sanction of the Government;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        arrange for the marketing of articles manufactured by small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        maintain depots for the supply of raw materials to and purchase of finished products from small and cottage industries and also maintain common facility centres to afford common facilities to small and cottage industries; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         prepare schemes to set up small industrial units in fields of high priority by itself or in collaboration with subsidiary corporations, public companies, partnership or persons execute them with the prior approval of the Government, and, after execution may transfer the ownership thereof for valuable consideration to any unit of subsidiary corporation, public company, partnership firm or persons, with the prior approval of, and on such terms as may be approved by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- Loans may by made by the Corporation in kind and may be in the form of factory buildings, residential houses or machinery equipment and raw materials on hire purchase basis 23[ ;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        prepare and implement investment schedules for small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h)        assist in setting up of small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         provide assistance to sick small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j) register shall and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(k)        collect, collate and analyse industrial date and establish date bank for small and cottage industries to assist the Government in the formulation of policy in the field of small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(l)         assist entrepreneurs with information relating to small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(m)       develop manufacturing process and technology for development of small and cottage industries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(n)        assist small and cottage industries in the matter of entering into contract and establishing business connections with medium and big industries for the purpose of supplying to them their products;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(o)        do such other acts and things as may be considered necessary for carrying out the purposes of this Act.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">24[ (3) Nothing in section 116 of the Companies Act, 1994 (Act 18 of 1994) shall apply to the Corporation.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Registration of small and cottage industries, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">25[ 24A. (1) Any person who has set up a small or cottage industry or intends to set up such industry and desires to have assistance and help from the Corporation shall apply to it, in such manner as may be prescribed by regulations, for registration of such industry.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An application for registration shall be allowed and the industry shall be registered if the Corporation is satisfied that the applicant has fulfilled all the conditions required for registration as may be prescribed by regulations.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) On the registration of an industry, the Corporation shall grant a certificate of registration to the applicant.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The registration of an industry may be cancelled by the Corporation if it is satisfied that the industry for which the registration was granted has ceased to exist or, as the case may be, has not been set up within the period of one year from the date of its registration.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The Corporation shall, on an application made by an industry registered under this section, give its decisions on all or any of the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        requirement of machinery, spare parts, components and raw materials;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        import entitlement in respect of machinery, spare parts, components and raw materials;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        terms and conditions of suppliers credits;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        terms and conditions of royalties, technical know-how and technical assistance fees;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        appointment of foreign personnel;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) allotment of land in the Corporation's estate.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) The Corporation shall, on an application made by an industry registered under this section, endeavour to facilitate the supply of electricity, water and gas and the providing of sewerage and telephone facilities within such time as may be agreed upon between the Corporation and the authorities or organizations concerned therewith.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power of the Corporation to enter into agreements with financial institutions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">24AA. The Corporation may enter into agreement with a financial institution in order that the latter may provide credit facilities to the small and cottage industries against adequate security subject to the condition that the losses and bad debts, if any, and the interest on the credit would be shared between the Corporation and the financial institution in the ratio agreed upon between them.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- In this section, “financial institution” means the Bangladesh Bank, Bangladesh Shilpa Bank, Bangladesh Shilpa Rin Sangstha, Bangladesh Krishi Bank, Rajshahi Krishi Unnayan Bank, any scheduled bank and a financial institution as defined in 26[ 2(j) of the Financial Institutions Act, 1993 (Act 27 of 1993).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">25. [Limit of accommodation.- Omitted by section 11 of the Bangladesh Small Industries Corporation (Amendment) Act, 1990 (Act No. LVII of 1990).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Security for loans or subscriptions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">26. No loan or subscription shall be made unless it is fully secured by pledge, mortgage, hypothecation or assignment of such property, movable or immovable, and of such value in proportion to the loan or subscription as may be prescribed:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that where the loan or subscription is made to an individual and does not exceed one thousand Taka in the aggregate, it may be secured by a bond with one surety.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Exemption from taxes</p><p style="text-align: justify;">27[ 26A. Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, exempt the Corporation in respect of any estate established by it or any small or cottage industry registered under this Act from payment of any tax, rate or toll payable under any law for the time being in force:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that no such exemption shall be granted unless the proposal for exemption is made by the Corporation.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Interest on loans</p><p style="text-align: justify;">27. The rate of interest chargeable on loans made by the Corporation shall be determined and notified by the Government from time to time.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">28. [Limits of loans.- Omitted by section 13 of the Bangladesh Small and Cottage Industries Corporation (Amendment) Act, 1990 (Act No. LVII of 1990). ]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to impose conditions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">29. (1) At the time of entering into any transaction under section 24, the Corporation may impose such conditions as it may think necessary or expedient for protecting its own interest and for securing that the loan, underwriting, subscription or other aid shall be put to the best use.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where aid is granted on the condition that a Director shall be appointed by the Corporation to the Board of a Company or a subsidiary Corporation or the Managing Committee of a Co-operative Society, such condition shall have effect notwithstanding anything contained in the 28[ Companies Act, 1994 (Act 18 of 1994)], or any other law for the time being in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Prohibited business</p><p style="text-align: justify;">30. The Corporation shall not -</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        accept deposits except as provided in or under this Act; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) subscribe directly to the shares or stock of any company having limited liability except with the previous permission of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Loans in foreign currency</p><p style="text-align: justify;">31. (1) For the purpose of granting a loan to any person in foreign currency, the Corporation may, with the previous consent of the Government 29[ * * *], borrow any such currency from the International Bank for Reconstruction and Development or Asian Development Bank or International Development Agency or from other sources, and may pledge, mortgage, hypothecate or assign to the said Bank or Agency or other lender all or any part of the security taken by the Corporation for the loan granted in foreign currency.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) [Omitted by section 14 of the Bangladesh Small and Cottage Industries Corporation (Amendment) Act, 1990 (Act No. LVII of 1990).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to demand immediate payment of the entire sum</p><p style="text-align: justify;">32. (1) Notwithstanding anything in any agreement, if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) it is found that the loan was obtained by information supplied by the borrower which was false or misleading in any material particular; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the borrower is found to have committed a breach of the terms of his agreement with the Corporation relating to the loan;
