274	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE ESSENTIAL SERVICES (SECOND) ORDINANCE, 1958 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE ESSENTIAL SERVICES (SECOND) ORDINANCE, 1958 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. XLI OF 1958).[16th July, 1958]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS by a Proclamation dated the 25th day of June, 1958, under Article 193 of the Constitution of the Islamic Republic of Pakistan, the President has assumed to himself all the powers vested in, or exercisable by the Governor of East Pakistan;           1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the President has, in pursuance of sub-clause (i) of clause (c) of the said Proclamation, been pleased to direct by notification No. 22/11/58-Pol. (I), dated the 4th July, 1958 published in the Extraordinary Gazette of Pakistan, dated the 4th July, 1958 that the powers vested in or exercisable by the Governor under the Constitution shall be exercised by the Governor;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS it is necessary to provide for powers for the maintenance of services essential to the life of the community and for the maintenance of public order;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the National Assembly is not in session and the Governor is satisfied that the circumstances exist which render it necessary for him to take immediate action;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by Article 102 of the Constitution of the Islamic Republic of Pakistan and of all other powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance, namely :-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Short title, extent and commencement</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 2[ * * *] Essential Services (Second) Ordinance, 1958.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 3[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Definition</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">“employment” includes employment of any nature whether paid or unpaid.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Application of the Ordinance</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. 4[ (1)] This Ordinance shall apply to all employments under the Government, and to such other employment or class of employment 5[ * * *], as the Government, being of the opinion that such employment or class of employment is essential for the maintenance of public order or for maintaining services necessary to the life of the community, may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare to be an employment or class of employment to which this Ordinance applies.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ (2) A declaration under sub-section (1) shall remain in force for a period of six months, but the Government may, by notification in official Gazette, successively extend it for further periods not exceeding six months at a time.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Offence</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. Any person engaged in any employment under the Government or in any employment or class of employment to which this Ordinance applies who,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        disobeys any lawful order given in course of such employment, or attempts to persuade any person to disobey any such order, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        without reasonable excuse abandons such employment or absents himself from work,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">shall be guilty of an offence under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ Explanation 1].- A person abandons his employment within the meaning of this section who, notwithstanding that it is an express or implied term of his contract of employment that he may terminate his employment on giving notice to his employer of his intention to do so, so terminates his employment without the previous consent of his employer.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[ Explanation 2.- Absence from work in pursuance of any notice of strike given or purported to be given under any law shall not be deemed to be a reasonable excuse within the meaning of this section.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Punishment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. Any person found guilty of an offence under this Ordinance shall be punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to one year or with fine or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Overriding Power of the Ordinance</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9[ 5A. The provisions of this Ordinance shall have effect notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained in the Industrial Relations Ordinance, 1969 (XXIII of 1969), or any other law for the time being in force.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Jurisdiction and mode of trial</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) No Magistrate other than a Magistrate of the first class shall try an offence under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Notwithstanding anything contained in the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, an offence under this Ordinance shall be cognizable.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Notwithstanding anything contained in the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, a Magistrate trying an offence under this Ordinance, shall have power to try such offence summarily and in trying such offences such Magistrates shall follow the procedure laid down in the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, for summary trial of summons cases.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[Repealed]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. [Repeal and saving.- Repealed by section 2 and the Schedule of the East Pakistan Repealing and Amending Ordinance, 1966 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. XIII of 1966).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by Article 8 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Bangladesh Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Bangladesh Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 Section 3 was renumbered as sub-section (1) by section 3 of the Essential Services Laws (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. XXXVI of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “under any local authority” were omitted by section 3 of the Essential Services Laws (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. XXXVI of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 Sub-section (2) was added by section 3 of the Essential Services Laws (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. XXXVI of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The Explanation was renumbered as Explanation 1 by section 3 of the Essential Services Laws (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. XXXVI of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 Explanation 2 was added by section 3 of the Essential Services Laws (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. XXXVI of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 Section 5A was added by section 3 of the Essential Services Laws (Amendment) Act, 1974 (Act No. XXXVI of 1974)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE CRIMINAL LAW AMENDMENT ACT, 1958 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ACT NO. XL OF 1958)[23rd  September, 1958]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 An Act to repeal and re-enact, with certain amendments, the 2[ Criminal Law] Amendment Act, 1948.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to repeal and re-enact, with certain amendments, the 3[ Criminal Law] Amendment Act, 1948, providing for the more speedy trial and more effective punishment of certain offences;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the 4[ Criminal Law] Amendment Act, 1958.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh and applies to all citizens of Bangladesh and public servants wherever they may be.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6[ (aa) “Commission” means Anti-Corruption Commission established under ???????? ??? ????? ???, ???? (???? ???? ??? ???)]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ (b) “public servant” means a public servant as defined in section 21 of the Penal Code (Act XLV of 1860), and includes a Chairman, Director, Trustee, Member, Commissioner, officer or other employee of any local authority, statutory corporation or body corporate or of any other body or organisation constituted or established under any law;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[ (bb) “Schedule” means Schedule of this Act;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) “Special Judge” means a Special Judge appointed under sub-section (1) of section 3.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appointment of Special Judges</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) The Government shall, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint as many Special Judges as may be necessary to try and punish offences specified in the Schedule.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9[ (2) No person shall be appointed a Special Judge unless he is or has been a Sessions Judge or an Additional Sessions Judge or an Assistant Sessions Judge 10[ * * *].]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Jurisdiction of Special Judges and cognizance of cases by them</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) A Special Judge shall have jurisdiction within such territorial limits as may be fixed by the Government by notification in the official Gazette and may take cognizance of any offence committed or deemed to have been committed within such limits and triable under this Act upon receiving a complaint of facts which constitute such offence or upon a report in writing of such facts made by any police officer.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where two or more Special Judges have jurisdiction, wholly or partly in the same territorial limits, the Government shall, by notification in the official Gazette, declare one of them to be the Senior Special Judge for that area 11[ ; and, notwithstanding anything contained in sub-section (1), such Senior Special Judge shall have exclusive jurisdiction to take cognizance of all offences triable under this Act committed or deemed to have been committed within that area.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) An offence shall be tried by the Special Judge within the territorial limits of whose jurisdiction it was committed or deemed to have been committed, or where there are more Special Judges than one having jurisdiction within the same territorial limits, 12[ by the Special Judge to whom the case is transferred] by the Senior Special Judge:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Senior Special Judge may, by order in writing, transfer, at any stage of the trial, any case from the Court of one Special Judge to the Court of another Special Judge having jurisdiction within the same territorial limits.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) When an offence triable under this Act is committed outside Bangladesh, it shall, for the purposes of this Act, be deemed to have been committed within the territorial limits of the jurisdiction of the Special Judge in which the person 13[ committing the offence is found or was ordinarily residing before he left Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">14[ (5) A Special Judge may pass any sentence authorised by law, except-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) a sentence of death or of imprisonment for life or of imprisonment for a term exceeding ten years, if he is or has been an Assistant Sessions Judge;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">15[ * * *]]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Offences to be tried by Special Judges</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, or in any other law, the offences specified in the Schedule shall be triable exclusively by a Special Judge.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) [Omitted by section 5 of the Criminal Law Amendment (Amendment) Act, 2004 (Act No. XXII of 2004).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) [Omitted by section 6 of the Criminal Law Amendment (Amendment) Ordinance, 1978 (Ordinance No. VI of 1978).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) [Omitted by section 5 of the Criminal Law Amendment (Amendment) Act, 2004 (Act No. XXII of 2004).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) In respect of cases transferred to a Special Judge under 16[ * * *] 17[ * * *] section 4 18[ * * *], such Judge shall not, by reason of the said transfer, be bound to recall and rehear any witness who has given evidence in the case before transfer and may act on the evidence already recorded by or produced before the court which tried the case before the transfer.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) For the purpose of trial 19[ under this Act,] a Special Judge may, in any case where he deems it necessary, order an investigation by 20[ the Commission].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7) When trying an offence under this Act a Special Judge may also charge with and try other offences not so triable with which the accused may, under the provisions of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, relating to the joinder of charges, be charged at the same trial.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Time-limit for investigation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">21[ 5A. Notwithstanding anything contained in the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898 (Act V of 1898), for the purpose of investigation of an offence triable under this Act, the offence shall be deemed to be an offence triable exclusively by Court of Sessions and the provisions of sub-section (5) of section 167 of that Code shall have effect as if for the words “sixty days” the words “one hundred and eighty days” were substituted.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Procedure in trial of cases and powers of Special Judges</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. 22[ (1) The provisions of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898 (Act V of 1898), shall, in so far as they are not inconsistent with this Act, apply to the proceedings of the Court of a Special Judge and for the purposes of the said provisions, the Court of a Special Judge shall be deemed to be-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        a Court of Sessions, if the Special Judge is or has been a Sessions Judge or an Additional Sessions Judge or an Assistant Sessions Judge.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">23[ * * *]]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">24[ (1A) If a Special Judge has reason to believe that an accused person has absconded or is concealing himself so that he cannot be arrested and produced before him for trial, he may, by order notified in the official Gazette, direct such person to appear before him within such period as may be specified in the order, and if such person fails to comply with such direction, he may be tried in his absence.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">25[ (1B) A person accused of more offences than one punishable under this Act may be tried at one trial for all such offences.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">26[ (2) Notwithstanding anything contained in the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898 (Act V of 1898), in the case of any offence specified in the Schedule, at any stage of investigation, enquiry, and trial the Special Judge, with a view to obtaining the evidence of any person supposed to have been directly or indirectly concerned in or privy to the offence, may for reasons to be recorded in writing tender pardon to such person on condition of his making a full and true disclosure of the whole of the circumstances within his knowledge relative to the offence and to every other person concerned, whether as principal or abettor, in the commission thereof and any pardon so tendered shall, for the purposes of sections 339 and 339A of the said Code, be deemed to have been tendered under section 337,or, as the case may be, under section 338 of that Code.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The provisions of Chapter XX of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, shall apply to trial of cases under this Act in so far as they are not inconsistent with the provisions of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Notwithstanding anything contained in this Act, the Special Judge may convict the accused of any offence which from the facts admitted or proved he appears to have committed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) [Omitted by section 6 of the Criminal Law Amendment (Amendment) Act, 2004 (Act No. XXII of 2004).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">27[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) [Omitted by section 6 of the Criminal Law Amendment (Amendment) Act, 2004 (Act No. XXII of 2004).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7) The previous statements of witnesses to be examined for the prosecution at the trial shall be supplied to the accused at least one week before the commencement of the trial.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Special rules of evidence</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. (1) When any person is charged before a Special Judge with an offence triable under this Act, the fact that such person or any other person through him or on his behalf, is in possession, for which he cannot satisfactorily account, of pecuniary resources, or property disproportionate to his known sources of income, or that such person has, on or about the time of offence with which he is charged, obtained an accretion to his pecuniary resources or property for which he cannot satisfactorily account, may be proved, and may be taken into consideration by the Special Judge as a relevant fact in deciding whether he is guilty of the particular offence with which he is charged.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where in any trial before a Special Judge of an offence punishable under sections 161 to 165 of the 28[ Penal Code], it is proved that an accused person has accepted or obtained, or has agreed to accept or attempted to obtain, for himself or for any other person, any gratification (other than legal remuneration) or any valuable thing, or any pecuniary advantage from a person or the agent of a person, for any favour shown or promised to be shown by the accused person, it shall be presumed, unless the contrary is proved, that he accepted or obtained, or agreed to accept or attempted to obtain, that gratification, or that valuable thing, or pecuniary advantage to himself or some other person, as the case may be, as a motive or reward such as is mentioned in sections 161, 162 and 163 of the 29[ Penal Code], or, as the case may be, without consideration, or for a consideration which he knows to be inadequate.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Where in any trial of an offence punishable under section 165A of the 30[ Penal Code], it is proved that any gratification (other than legal remuneration) or any valuable thing has been given or offered to be given or attempted to be given by an accused person, it shall be presumed unless the contrary is proved that he gave or offered to give or attempted to give the gratification or valuable thing, as the case may be, as a motive or reward such as is mentioned in section 161 of the said Code or, as the case may be, without consideration or for a consideration which he knew to be inadequate.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Notwithstanding anything contained in sub-sections (2) and (3), the Court may decline to draw the presumption referred to in either of the said sub-sections, if the gratification or thing aforesaid is, in its opinion, so trivial that no inference of corruption may fairly be drawn.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Bar on trial de novo</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. A Special Judge, unless he otherwise decides, shall not be bound to recall or rehear any witness, whose evidence has already been recorded, or to re-open proceedings already held, but may act on the evidence already produced or recorded and continue the trial from the stage which the case has reached.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Punishment of offences</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. When any person charged before a Special Judge with an offence triable under this Act is found guilty of the offence the Special Judge shall, notwithstanding anything contained in any other law, whether or not he imposes a sentence of imprisonment, impose a sentence of fine which shall not be less than the gain found to have been derived by the accused by the 31[ commission of the offence and may also order confiscation of the whole or any part of the property of the accused to the Government].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appeal, revision and transfer of cases</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. 32[ (1) An appeal from the judgement of a Special Judge shall lie to-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the High Court Division, if the Special Judge is or has been a Sessions Judge or an Additional Sessions Judge or an Assistant Sessions Judge;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">33[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(1A) The Court to which an appeal lies under sub-section (1) shall also have powers of revisions.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Notwithstanding the provisions of section 417 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, in any case tried by a Special Judge appointed by the Government under section 3, in which such Special Judge has passed an order of acquittal, 34[ the Commission may] direct the Public Prosecutor to present an appeal to such Court as aforesaid.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The 35[ High Court Division] shall have authority to transfer any case from the Court of a Special Judge to the Court of another Special Judge:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that notwithstanding anything contained in section 526 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, the Special Judge from whose Court a transfer is desired, shall not be bound to adjourn the case, but if he rejects a request for adjournment, he shall record his reasons for doing so.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) No prosecution under this Act against any person either generally or in respect of any one or more of the offences for which he is being tried shall be withdrawn except under the orders in writing of the 36[ Commission].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Bail and imprisonment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in the Second Schedule to the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, or any other law for the time being in force, offences triable by a Special Judge under this Act shall be deemed to be non-bailable.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Any offence triable under this Act which is punishable with simple imprisonment shall be deemed to be punishable with imprisonment of either description.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. (1) The Government may frame rules to carry out the purposes of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular, and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing powers, such rules may provide for any of the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">37[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the emoluments of the Special Judges, and their appointment;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        territorial limits of the jurisdiction of Special Judges and the place and time of sitting of the Courts presided over by the Special Judges;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) the summoning of witnesses and compelling the production of documents and the penalty for disobeying, or evading the same, in addition to or substitution of the provisions of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) matters incidental to the above.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Military, naval and air force law not to be affected</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. Nothing in this Act shall affect the jurisdiction exercised by, or the procedure applicable to, any Court or other authority under any military, naval, or air force law.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. [Repeal and savings.- Omitted by section 9 of the Criminal Law Amendment (Amendment) Ordinance, 1978 (Ordinance No. VI of 1978).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, the words “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted 275	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE EYE SURGERY (RESTRICTION) ORDINANCE, 1960 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"><strong>THE EYE SURGERY (RESTRICTION) ORDINANCE, 1960</strong></p><p align="center">(ORDINANCE NO. LI OF 1960)</p><p align="right">[31st December, 1960]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to prevent surgery on the eye by persons other than registered medical practitioners. 1</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to prevent surgery on the eye by persons other than registered medical practitioners;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the seventh day of October 1958, and in exercise of the powers conferred by Article 2 of the State Arrangements Order, 1959, and of all other powers enabling him in that behalf, the Minister exercising the functions of President under the said Article makes and promulgates the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the Eye Surgery (Restriction) Ordinance, 1960.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(1)        “complete blindness” means absence of sight through total loss of perception of light in both eyes;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2)        “eye surgery” means any surgical operation performed on or in relation to the eye by means of any instrument of whatever kind;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3)        “partial blindness” means total loss of perception of light in one eye or sub-total loss of perception of light in both eyes resulting in restriction of visual field and acuity; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4)        “registered medical practitioner” means a person who is, for the time being, registered under any law relating to the registration of medical practitioners in Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Punishment for performing eye surgery in certain cases</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) Any person, not being a registered medical practitioner, who performs eye surgery upon another, whether with or without the latter's consent, shall be punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to one year, and with fine which may extend to one thousand taka.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The term of imprisonment under sub-section (1) may extend-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        to three years, if the offence results in partial blindness, and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        to seven years , if the offence results in complete blindness.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Punishment for unlawful practice or holding out</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. Any person not being a registered medical practitioner who practises, or holds himself out, whether directly or by implication, as practising, or as being prepared to practise, eye surgery shall be punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to six months, and with fine which may extend to five hundred taka.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Offences to be cognizable</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. An offence punishable under sub-section (1) of section 3 or under section 4 shall be a cognizable offence for the purposes of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained therein.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Trial of offences</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. No court inferior to that of a Magistrate of the first class shall try any offence punishable under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">_______________________________________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the words “Bangladesh” and “taka” were substituted for the words “Pakistan” and “rupees” respectively by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973).</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
276	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE FILM DEVELOPMENT CORPORATION ACT, 1957 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE FILM DEVELOPMENT CORPORATION ACT, 1957 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ACT NO. XV OF 1957)[21st  May, 1957]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An  Act to establish a Corporation for the purpose of promoting the development of film industry in Bangladesh.             1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Whereas it is expedient to establish a Corporation for the purpose of promoting the development of film industry in Bangladesh;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the 2[ * * *] Film Development Corporation Act, 1957.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force on such date as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, appoint.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Interpretation </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “Board” means the Board of Directors of the Corporation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “Borrower” means any person or persons or body of persons, whether incorporated or not, to whom a loan is made by the Corporation under this Act and the successors and assignees of such person or persons;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “Corporation” means the Film Development Corporation established by this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “Film industry” means an industry engaged in the production of motion pictures for commercial exhibition and includes the setting up and maintaining of studios for the production of films;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) “Film” means celluloid film used for producing motion pictures for commercial exhibition;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3[ (f)    “Scheduled Bank” means a Bank for the time being included in the list of Banks maintained under clause (1) of Article 37 of the Bangladesh Bank Order, 1972 (P.O. No. 127 of 1972)]; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Establishment and incorporation of Corporation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) A Corporation to be called “The Film Development Corporation” shall be established as soon as may be after the commencement of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Corporation shall be a body corporate by the name of the Film Development Corporation, having perpetual succession and a common seal, with power, subject to the provisions of this Act, to acquire and hold property, both movable and immovable, and shall by the said name sue and be sued.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Share capital and shareholders</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) The authorised capital of the Corporation shall, in the first instance, be one crore of taka, divided into ten lakh fully paid up shares of Tk 10 each. These shares may be issued and allotted by the Corporation from time to time with the previous sanction of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The authorised capital may, with the previous approval of the Government, be increased from time to time by the Corporation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Government shall be a shareholder of the Corporation and shall subscribe to and hold not less than fifty-one per centum of the shares issued by the Corporation at any time; the remaining shares shall be reserved for public subscription.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Approved securities</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. The shares and debentures of the Corporation shall be deemed to be “approved securities” for the purposes of the Trusts Act, 1882.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Management</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) The general direction and administration of the Corporation and its affairs shall vest in a Board of Directors, which, with the assistance of an Executive Committee and a Managing Director, may exercise all powers and do all acts and things, which may be exercised or done by the Corporation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Board in discharging its functions shall act on commercial considerations and shall be guided on questions of policy by such directions as the Government, which shall be the sole judge whether a question is a question of policy, may direct from time to time.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) If the Board fails to carry out any direction given as aforesaid, the Government may remove the Directors, including the Chairman with the exception of Directors elected under section 7(b) for reasons to be recorded in writing, and, notwithstanding anything in section 7, appoint persons in their place to be Directors temporarily until a fresh Board is constituted in accordance with the provisions of that section.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Board of Directors</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. The Board of Directors shall consist of the following, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        four Directors to be appointed by the Government; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        not more than three Directors to be elected in the prescribed manner by the shareholders of the Corporation other than the Government at any time being determined in accordance with the following table:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        The Managing Director to be appointed by the Government under section 9:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that when the Board is first constituted the Directors referred to in clause (b) shall be appointed by the Government in accordance with the table given in the said clause from amongst the shareholders and shall, for the purpose of this Act, be deemed to be elected Directors.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Terms of office of Directors</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. (1) A Director appointed by the Government shall hold office during the pleasure of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An elected Director shall hold office for a period of three years, shall continue in office after the expiry of his term until his successor is elected, and shall be eligible for re-election.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) A casual vacancy in the office of the Director shall be filled by election or appointment, as the case may be, and the Director elected or appointed to fill the vacancy shall hold office for the unexpired period of the term of his predecessor:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that it shall not be necessary to fill a casual vacancy occurring within three months of the end of the term in which it occurs.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) No act or proceeding of the Board shall be invalid merely on the ground of the existence of any vacancy in, or any defect in the composition of, the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Managing Director</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. The Managing Director shall be appointed by the Government and shall -</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        perform such duties as the Board may by regulations assign to him;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        divest himself of any directorship in any other corporation, company or concern;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        hold office, unless removed earlier by the Government, for a term of three years and shall be eligible for re-appointment for a further term or terms:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that any such further term may be for such period not exceeding three years as the Government may determine; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        be entitled to receive such salary and allowances as the Government may determine.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Constitution and powers of the Executive Committee</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10.       (1) The Executive Committee shall consist of three members, that is to say, the Managing Director (who shall be the Chairman of the Committee), one Director appointed by the Government from amongst the appointed Directors and one Director elected from amongst the elected Directors in the prescribed manner by the shareholders of the Corporation other than the Government:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        if there is only one elected Director at any time, he shall be deemed to have been elected as a member;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        if there is no elected Director at any time, the membership reserved for elected Directors shall be filled, until such time as a Director is elected, by a Director appointed by the Government from amongst the appointed Directors.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An elected member shall hold office for three years and shall be eligible for re-election, but shall cease to hold office when he ceases to be an elected Director.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Subject to such general or special directions as may from time to time be given by the Board, the Executive Committee shall be competent to deal with any matter within the competence of the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The minutes of every meeting of the Executive Committee shall be laid before the Board at its next following meeting.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Disqualification for the office of Director</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11. No person shall be or shall continue to be a Director who-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        is a salaried official of the Corporation other than the Managing Director, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        is or at any time has been adjudicated insolvent, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) is found to be lunatic or of unsound mind, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        is or at any time has been convicted of an offence which in the opinion of the Government is an offence involving moral turpitude, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        is a minor.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Directors absent from three consecutive meetings</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12. A person shall cease to be a Director if he absents from three consecutive meetings of the Board without leave of absence from the Chairman, or, in the case of the Chairman, from the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appointment of officers, advisers and consultants</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13. The Corporation may, subject to such instructions as may be issued by the Government in this behalf, appoint or employ such persons, including advisers and consultants, as it considers necessary for the efficient performance of its functions.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Chairman of the Board</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14. (1) The Government shall appoint one of the Directors other than the Managing Director to be the Chairman of the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Subject to his continuing to hold office as a Director, the Chairman shall hold office as Chairman for a term of three years and thereafter until his successor is appointed and shall be eligible for re-appointment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Technical Advisory Committee</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15. The Corporation shall appoint a Committee of experts to be called “The Technical Advisory Committee” to give it technical advice on schemes submitted to the Corporation for financial assistance or on any point that may be referred to the Committee by the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Restriction on disclosure of information</p><p style="text-align: justify;">16. No information given by a person applying for financial assistance and made known to the Committee shall be disclosed or used by any member of the Committee without the written consent of such person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Meetings of the Board and the Committee and quorum thereof</p><p style="text-align: justify;">17. (1) The meetings of the Board and the Executive Committee shall be held at such times and at such places as may be prescribed by rules:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that until rules are made in this behalf such meetings shall be convened by the Chairman of the Board or the Committee, as the case may be.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) To constitute a quorum at a meeting of-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        the Board, not less than three Directors shall be present;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the Executive Committee, not less than two members shall be present.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) At a meeting of the Board or of the Executive Committee, each Director or member of the Committee, as the case may be, shall have one vote, and in the event of equality of votes the Chairman shall have a casting vote.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) No Director shall vote on any matter relating to an industrial concern in which he is directly or indirectly interested.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) If for any reason the Chairman is unable to be present at a meeting-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        of the Board, a Director other than the Managing Director authorised in writing by the Chairman shall preside at that meeting and in default of such authorisation the Directors present may elect a Chairman to preside at that meeting;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        of the Executive Committee, a member authorised in writing by the Managing Director shall preside at that meeting and in default of such authorisation the members present may elect a Chairman to preside at that meeting.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Fees for attending meetings</p><p style="text-align: justify;">18. Directors other than the Managing Director and not being servants of the Government shall be paid such fees for attending the meetings of the Board or the Executive Committee, if they are members of it, as may be prescribed by the Board.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Offices</p><p style="text-align: justify;">19. The Corporation shall establish its Head Office in 6[ Dhaka].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Deposit accounts</p><p style="text-align: justify;">20. The Corporation may open a deposit account with the 7[ Sonali Bank] or with such other Scheduled Bank as the Government may approve.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Investment of funds</p><p style="text-align: justify;">21. The Corporation may invest its funds in such securities or in such other manner as may be prescribed by rules.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Borrowing power</p><p style="text-align: justify;">22. (1) The Corporation, with the prior approval of the Government, may issue and sell bonds and debentures carrying interest at such rates as may be approved by the Government for the purpose of raising its working capital:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the total of sums due on such bonds and debentures issued and outstanding and of the contingent liabilities of the Corporation in respect of guarantees or underwriting agreements shall not at any time exceed five times the combined amount of the paid-up share capital and the reserve fund of the Corporation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The bonds and debentures of the Corporation shall be guaranteed by the Government as to the repayment of principal and payment of interest at such rate as may be fixed by the Government at the time when the bonds and debentures are issued.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Deposits</p><p style="text-align: justify;">23. The Corporation may accept deposits on such terms and conditions and to such extent as may be approved by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Functions of the Corporation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">24. (1) The Corporation shall take such measures as it thinks fit to render assistance in the development of film industry.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing power, the Corporation may, in order to carry out the purposes of this Act,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        give loans to persons or companies for producing motion pictures, and establishment and maintenance of studios;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        give loans to persons or corporations for setting up film studios;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        set up studios itself and to make available the use of such studios on hire to film producers:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the loans given or guaranteed under clauses (a) and (b) shall be repayable within a period not exceeding three years;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        prepare and submit to the Government schemes for the development of film industry and small-scale industries, including schemes of research in connection thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        import cinematograph films and other necessary requisites for production or processing of films for distribution to film producers;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         give loans to motion picture exhibitors for purchase of projectors and ancillaries thereto.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">This shall not include loans for lands, construction of buildings and fittings and furnishings.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Explanation.- Loans may be given by the Corporation in kind and may include letting of its studios on hire.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[ (3) Nothing in section 116 of Companies Act, 1994 (Act 18 of 1994) shall apply to the Corporation.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Limit of accommodation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">25. The Corporation shall not grant or make any such loan as is mentioned in clause (a) or clause (b) or clause (f) of sub-section (2) of section 24 to an extent which in the aggregate exceeds 10 per centum of the paid-up share capital:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that in individual cases the limit of ten per centum may be relaxed by the Government for special reasons on the recommendation of the Corporation, but in no case shall the amount of any loan exceed three lakhs of taka.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Security for loans</p><p style="text-align: justify;">26. No loan shall be made unless it is fully secured by pledge, mortgage, hypothecation or assignment of such property, movable or immovable, and of such value in proportion to the loan as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Interest on loans</p><p style="text-align: justify;">27. The rate of interest chargeable on loans made by the Corporation shall be determined and notified by the Government from time to time.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Limit of loans</p><p style="text-align: justify;">28. The Corporation shall not make loans in excess of the following aggregate limits, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        when made to an individual -Tk 50,000.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        when made to a company - Tk 1,00,000:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the above limits may be relaxed by the Government in special cases for special reasons on the recommendation of the Corporation subject to the limit prescribed in the proviso to section 25.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to impose conditions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">29. (1) At the time of entering into any transaction under section 24, the Corporation may impose such conditions as it may think necessary or expedient for protecting its own interest and for securing that the loan, underwriting or other aid shall be put to the best use.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where aid is granted on the condition that a Director shall be appointed by the Corporation to the Board of a Company, such condition shall have effect notwithstanding anything contained in the 9[ Companies Act, 1994 (Act 18 of 1994)], or any other law for the time being in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Prohibited business</p><p style="text-align: justify;">30. The Corporation shall not-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        accept deposits except as provided in or under this Act; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        subscribe directly to the shares or stock of any company having limited liability.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Loans in foreign currency</p><p style="text-align: justify;">31. (1) For the purpose of granting a loan to an individual or a company in foreign currency, the Corporation may, with the previous consent of the Government 10[ * * *], borrow any such currency from the International Bank for Reconstruction and Development or from other sources, and may pledge, mortgage, hypothecate or assign to the said Bank or other lender all or any part of the security taken by the Corporation for the loan granted in foreign currencies.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) All loans granted in foreign currency shall be repayable either-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) in the currency in which they are granted, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        in 11[ Bangladesh] currency at the rate of exchange prevailing on the date of repayment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to demand immediate payment of the entire sum</p><p style="text-align: justify;">32. (1) Notwithstanding anything in any agreement, if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) it is found that the loan was obtained by information supplied by the borrower which was false or misleading in any material particular; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the borrower is found to have committed a breach of the terms of his agreement with the Corporation relating to the loan; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        the loan or any part of it is found to have been utilised otherwise than for the purpose for which it was made; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        there is a reasonable apprehension that the borrower will be unable to pay his debts or may go into liquidation; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        the property pledged, mortgaged, hypothecated or assigned to the Corporation as security for the loan is not kept in a proper condition by the borrower or in case the property has depreciated in value by more than the prescribed percentage and the borrower is unable to give additional security to the satisfaction of the Corporation; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         without the permission of the Board the house, land or other property mortgaged as security for the loan is in any way disposed of or charged by the borrower; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        without the permission of the Board, machinery or other equipment is removed from the premises of the borrower's establishment without being replaced; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h)        for any other reason, it is necessary in the opinion of the Board to do so in order to protect the interests of the Corporation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">any officer of the Board authorised generally or specially in this behalf by the Board may by notice call upon the borrower to pay up the entire sum then remaining unpaid by the borrower in respect of the loan and the interest payable thereon, or any lesser sum, or require the borrower to comply with such directions as the Board may consider it necessary to give in order to safeguard its interest.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Such notice shall specify the time within which the borrower was required to make the payment or to carry out the directions given, and shall also contain a warning that, if the borrower fails to pay the amount demanded or to carry out the directions given within the time specified, the Board may issue a certificate certifying the borrower to be a defaulter and certifying the sum due from the borrower to be recoverable as arrears of land revenue.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Certification of sums recoverable</p><p style="text-align: justify;">33.       (1) If the borrower fails to make the payment demanded or to carry out the directions given in a notice under section 32 within the time specified in the notice, the Board may issue a certificate in the prescribed form and manner certifying the borrower to be a defaulter and certifying the aggregate sum, including interest, payable by the borrower to the Corporation on and up to the date of the certificate and the rate at which interest was payable thereon thereafter.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Subject to the provisions of sub-section (3), a certificate issued under sub-section (1) shall be conclusive evidence that the sums certified in the certificate together with further interest at the rate certified were recoverable by the Corporation from the borrower, and such sums shall be immediately recoverable as arrears of land revenue.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The borrower may appeal to the Government against a certificate issued under sub-section (1) within 15 days of its issue and the Government may cancel or modify the certificate.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Special provisions for enforcement of the claims of the Corporation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">34.       (1) When a certificate under section 33 has been issued and is subsisting against a borrower, any officer nominated for this purpose by the Corporation may file a suit by presenting a plaint in the prescribed manner in the Court within the local limits of whose jurisdiction the loan was made or the establishment or concern in respect of which the loan was made or any immovable property charged as security was situated for any one or more or all of the following reliefs, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) an order for the recovery of the amount due to the Corporation executable personally against the borrower and by a
