Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p>                       </div></div>
280	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE GOVERNMENT FISHERIES (PROTECTION) ORDINANCE, 1959 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"><strong>THE GOVERNMENT FISHERIES (PROTECTION) ORDINANCE, 1959</strong></p><p align="center">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. XXIV OF 1959)</p><p align="right">[24th March, 1959]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to make provisions for preventing unauthorised fishing in fisheries belonging to, or under the management and control of, the Government;    1</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Presidential Proclamation of the 7th day of October, 1958, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor of East Pakistan is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 2[ * * *] Government Fisheries (Protection) Ordinance, 1959.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 3[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “Khas managed fishery” means a fishery declared by the Government under section 3 to be a Khas managed fishery;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) “prescribed” means prescribed by rules made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Declaration of a fishery to be a khas managed fishery</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare any fishery belonging to, or under the management and control of, the Government to be a khas managed fishery.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Bar to unauthorised fishing in khas managed fisheries</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) On the declaration of a fishery to be a khas managed fishery under section 3, no person shall fish in such a fishery without a valid licence for fishing issued by such authority as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It shall be competent for the Government or any authority authorised by the Government to fix different rates of licence fees for fishing in a khas managed fishery with different varieties of fishing contrivances or by using different methods of fishing and to lay down the terms and conditions of any license.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Carrying of valid licence of fishing and production of the same</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. Every person fishing in any manner or carrying any fishing contrivance in a khas managed fishery shall carry with him a valid licence for fishing in such manner or with such contrivance and produce the same when required by such person or class of persons as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Bar to unauthorised fishing in other fisheries</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. No person shall fish or attempt to fish in any fishery, other than khas managed fishery, belonging to, or under the management and control of, the Government or enter into any such fishery for the purpose of fishing or causing fishing to be done, without the authority of the Government or of any lessee of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Authorisation by Government to question illegal fishing</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, authorise any person or class of persons,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) to detain and search any boat found in any fishery belonging to, or under the management and control of, the Government and seize the boat with the fishing contrivance used or carried without valid licence or authority;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        to search any place where fish caught or fishing contrivances used or carried without a valid licence or authority are reasonably suspected to be found and seize such fish or contrivances;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        to seize any fish caught in contravention of the provisions of this Ordinance; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) to require any person found fishing or attempting to fish in any fishery belonging to, or under the management and control of, the Government to state truly his name, his father's name and address and to produce his authority for such fishing.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Exemption</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. Nothing in this Ordinance shall apply to carrying of fishing contrivances in a boat or ship plying as a public carrier on a regulated route or to fishing with line and rod, basket or kotch for personal consumption.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Penal clauses</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. (1) Contravention of any provision of this Ordinance or any rules made thereunder shall, on conviction by a Court of competent jurisdiction, be punishable with imprisonment which may extend to 2 years or with fine which may extend to 4[ Tk] 5,000 or with both and any fish or fishing contrivance including any boat may be forfeited to the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) An offence under this Ordinance shall be cognizable and bailable.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Rule-making power</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">__________________________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Tk” was substituted for the words “Rs.” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
281	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">   THE HATS AND BAZARS (ESTABLISHMENT AND ACQUISITION) ORDINANCE, 1959 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>THE HATS AND BAZARS (ESTABLISHMENT AND ACQUISITION) ORDINANCE, 1959 </strong></p><p style="text-align: center;">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. XIX OF 1959)</p><p style="text-align: right;">[2nd March, 1959]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to control the establishment of hats and bazars and acquire certain hats and bazars already established. 1</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to make provisions for controlling the establishment of hats and bazars in Bangladesh and for the acquisition of the hats and bazars established after the final publication of the Compensation Assessment roll under section 42 of the 2[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Presidential Proclamation of the 7th day of October, 1958 and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 3[ * * *] Hats and Bazars (Establishment and Acquisition) Ordinance, 1959.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Establishment of Hats and Bazars</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. (1) No person shall establish any hat or bazar in Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Nothing in sub-section (1) shall prevent the Government or any local authority from establishing any hat or bazar:</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that prior approval of the Deputy Commissioner shall, in the case of a local authority, be necessary.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4[ Explanation:- In sub-section (2), “local authority” shall have same meaning as defined in clause 28 of section 3 of the General Clauses Act, 1897 (X of 1897), or any other authority legally entitled to, or entrusted by the Government with, the control of management of a local fund.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Any hat or bazar established in contravention of the provisions of sub-sections (1) and (2) including the land on which such hat or bazar is established and all interests therein shall be forfeited to the Government:</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that where any hat or bazar has been so established on any land by a person or persons other than the owner of the land without the consent of such owner, the land shall not be forfeited, but it shall be lawful for the Deputy Commissioner,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i)         to remove the hat or bazar from the land, by using such force as may be necessary, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) to take over the land on behalf of the Government on payment to the owner the market value of the land immediately before the establishment of the hat or bazar to be determined in the manner prescribed by the rules, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       to issue a licence to the owner permitting him to continue the hat or bazar for such period and on payment of such fees and on such terms and conditions as may be prescribed by rules.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Power of the Government to acquire hats and bazars and determination of compensation</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in any other law for the time being in force, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, acquire with effect from such date as may be specified in that notification, any hat or bazar established in any area after the final publication of the Compensation Assessment-roll under section 42 of the 5[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, in respect of that area, on payment of compensation at the rate provided for in clause (b) of sub-section (1) of section 39 of the said Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) On and from the date specified in the notification under sub-section (1) in respect of any hat or bazar, such hat or bazar shall vest in the Government free from all encumbrances.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The compensation payable under sub-section (1) shall be determined and paid to person or persons interested by the Deputy Commissioner in such manner as may be prescribed by rules made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) An appeal against the order of the Deputy Commissioner under sub-section (3), if preferred within 30 days of the date of the order, shall lie to the 6[ Commissioner of the Division].</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ (4a) An order of the Commissioner passed under sub-section (4) and, subject only to such order, an order of the Deputy Commissioner passed under sub-section (3) shall be final.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) [Omitted by the Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Repealing and Amending) Order, 1973 (President's Order No. 12 of 1973).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Interpretation</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. For the purpose of this Ordinance, the expression “Deputy Commissioner” shall include an Additional Deputy Commissioner and a Joint Deputy Commissioner and all other words and expressions used in this Ordinance and defined in the 8[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, shall have meanings respectively assigned to them by that Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Rule-making power</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">_____________________________________________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the word “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted for the words “East Pakistan” and “Provincial Government” respectively by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Bangal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The Explanation was substituted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The words “Commissioner of the Division” were substituted for the words “Civil Court” by section 2 and the Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws ( Amending) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. IX of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 Sub-section (4a) was inserted by section 2 and the Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Amending) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. IX of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p> </div></div>
282	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE INLAND WATER TRANSPORT AUTHORITY ORDINANCE, 1958 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE INLAND WATER TRANSPORT AUTHORITY ORDINANCE, 1958 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. LXXV OF 1958).[31st October, 1958]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 An Ordinance to set up an Authority for development, maintenance and control of inland water transport and of certain inland navigable waterways 2[ * * *].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is necessary to make provisions for setting up of an Authority for the development, maintenance and control of inland water transport and of certain inland navigable waterways in 3[ Bangladesh];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the Provincial Assembly of East Pakistan has been dissolved with the abrogation of the Constitution by the Proclamation of the President on 7th October, 1958;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the Governor of a Province has been vested with the powers of promulgating Ordinance as if clauses (1) and (3) of Article 102 of the late Constitution are still in force;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in exercise of the powers conferred by clause (1) of Article 5 of the Laws (Continuance in Force) Order, 1958, promulgated by the President of Pakistan on the 10th October, 1958 and of all other powers enabling him in that behalf the Governor of East Pakistan is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Short title, extent and commencement</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1.         (1) This Ordinance may be called the 4[ * * *] Inland Water Transport Authority Ordinance, 1958.        (2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Definitions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2.         In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) “Authority” means the Bangladesh Inland Water Transport Authority established under section 3 of this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) “Chairman” means the Chairman appointed under section 4 of this Ordinance; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       “Prescribed” means prescribed by rule made under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Establishment and Incorporation of Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3.         (1) The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, establish an Authority to be known as the Bangladesh Inland Water Transport Authority for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5[ (2) The Authority shall be a body corporate, having perpetual succession and a common seal, with power, subject to the provisions of this Ordinance, and any other law for the time being in force, to acquire, hold and dispose of, by lien, mortgage, sale, alienation or otherwise, property, both movable and immovable, and shall by the said name sue and be sued.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appointment and term of office of Chairman and Members</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4.          6[ (1) The Authority shall consist of a Chairman and such number of members as the Government may, from time to time, determine.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7[ (1A) The Chairman and Members of the Authority shall be the whole time Officers of the Authority and shall be appointed by the Government on such terms and conditions as it may determine.]]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The term of office of the Chairman shall be five years and that of a member three years.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) [Omitted by section 3 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) Any person ceasing to be the Chairman or member by reason of the expiry of the term of his office shall be eligible for re-appointment for another term or for such shorter term as the Government may decide.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The Chairman or any member may at any time resign:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that his resignation shall not take effect until accepted by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) In the case of temporary absence of the Chairman or any member, the Government may appoint a Chairman or a member, as the case may be, for the period of absence.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Remuneration and conditions of service</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. The Chairman and each member shall receive such salary and allowances and be subject to such conditions of service as may be prescribed by the Government, and shall perform such duties as are assigned to them under this Ordinance or by any rules framed under it.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Removal of Chairman or Members</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, remove the Chairman or any member-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) if he refuses or fails to discharge or becomes, in the opinion of the Government, incapable of discharging his responsibilities under this Ordinance; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        if he has been declared insolvent; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        if he has been declared to be disqualified for employment in, or has been dismissed from the service of 8[ the Republic], or has been convicted of an offence involving moral turpitude; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        if he has knowingly acquired or continued to hold without the permission in writing of the Government, directly or indirectly or through a partner, any share or interest in any contract or employment with or by or on behalf of the Authority, or in any land or property which, in his knowledge, is likely to benefit him or has benefited him as a result of the operation of the Authority.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Meetings of Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7.         (1) The Authority shall meet at such time and place and in such manner, as may be prescribed:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that until rules are made in this behalf, such meetings shall be convened by the Chairman.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Chairman, or in his absence a member authorised by him, and one other member shall be present to constitute a quorum at a meeting of the Authority.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Chairman shall have power to vote in a meeting of the Authority and in the case of equality of votes he shall have a casting vote also.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Advisory Committee</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. 9[ (1) The Government may constitute, as and when it considers necessary so to do, an Advisory Committee consisting of the Chairman who shall also be the Chairman of the Committee and such number of other members as the Government may deem fit.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Secretary of the Authority shall act as the Secretary of the Advisory Committee.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Advisory Committee shall meet at least once in every three months and the meetings of the Advisory Committee shall be called by the Chairman.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The members of the Advisory Committee shall be entitled to such fees and allowances as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The Advisory Committee may advise the Authority in respect of all matters relating to the development, maintenance and operation of inland water transport and of inland waterways in Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) [Omitted by section 7 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Powers of the Government to supersede the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. If, in the opinion of the Government, the Authority have shown their incompetency, to perform or have persistently made default in the performance of the duties imposed on them by or under this Ordinance or have exceeded or abused their powers, the Government may, by an order published in the official Gazette, supersede them for a period specified in the order:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Government before six months of such order or supersession shall give notice to the Authority to show cause why such action shall not be taken and also to provide them an opportunity to take remedial measures:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided further that except in case of misappropriation of Authority funds or persistent default in the performance of duties by the Authority the Government shall not ordinarily exercise powers under this section.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Temporary association of members with the Authority for particular purposes</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10.       (1) The Authority may associate with themselves any person whose assistance or advice they may desire in carrying out any of the provisions of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A person associated with themselves by the Authority under sub-section (1) for any purpose shall have a right to take part in the discussions of the Authority.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Sub-Committees</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11.       The Authority may constitute sub-committees from amongst the members of the Advisory Committee constituted under section 8 and associated members under section 10 of this Ordinance to study and advise on the specific local requirements.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Determination of number, designation, etc, of officers and servants of the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12.       The Authority may, subject to such conditions as may be prescribed, determine the number, designation and grade of officers and servants whom the Authority consider necessary to employ for the purpose of this Ordinance and the amount and nature of salary and allowances to be paid to each such officer and servant.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power of appointment, suspension, etc, of officers and servants of the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13.       The power of appointing, promoting and granting leave to officers and servants of the Authority and reducing in rank, suspending and dismissing them for misconduct, shall, subject to such conditions as may be prescribed, be vested in the Authority.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Transfer of Officers on deputation</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10[ 13A. Notwithstanding anything contained in this Ordinance or in any other law, rule or regulation for the time being in force, the Government may, if it considers necessary in the public interest, transfer on deputation any Officer of the Authority to Chittagong Port Authority established under the Chittagong Port Authority Ordinance, 1976 (LII of 1976) and Mongla Port Authority established under the Mongla Port Authority Ordinance, 1976 (LIII of 1976) and vice versa.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Delegation of powers to Chairman, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11[ 14. The Authority may by general or special order, delegate to Chairman or a Member or an Officer of the Authority any of its powers, duties or functions under this Ordinance subject to such conditions as it may think fit to impose.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Functions of the Authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15.       (1) The Authority may perform any or all of the following functions, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) carry out river conservancy works including river training works for navigational purposes and for provision of aids to navigation, including marks, buoys, lights and semaphore signals;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        disseminate navigational and meteorological information including publishing river charts;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       maintain pilotage and hydrographic survey services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       draw up programmes of dredging requirements and priorities for efficient maintenance of existing navigable waterways, and for resuscitation of dead or dying rivers, channels, or canals, including development of new channels and canals for navigation;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v)        develop, maintain and operate inland river ports, landing ghats and terminal facilities in such ports or ghats;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vi)       carry out removal of wrecks and obstructions in inland navigable waterways;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vii)      conduct traffic surveys to establish passenger and cargo requirements on the main rivers, feeders and creek routes;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(viii) develop the most economical facilities for passenger traffic to ensure comfort, safety and speed on mechanised craft;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ix)       fix maximum and minimum fares and freight rates for Inland Water Transport on behalf of the Government as provided in 12[ section 59 of the Inland Shipping Ordinance, 1976];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(x)        approve time-tables for passenger services;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xi)       develop rural water transport by progressing of schemes for modernising and mechanising country craft;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xii) ensure co-ordination of Inland Water Transport with other forms of transport, with major sea ports, and with trade and agricultural interests for the optimum utilisation of the available transport capacity;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xiii) conduct research in matters relating to Inland Water Transport including development of-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        craft design,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        technique of towage,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        landing and terminal facilities,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        port installations;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xiv) arrange programmes of technical training for Inland Water Transport personnel within and outside 13[ Bangladesh];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xv)      maintain liaison with the shipyard and ship repair industry to meet the requirements of the Inland Water Transport fleet repairs and new constructions;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xvi) 14[ * * *] facilitate import of repair materials for the Inland Water Transport Industry;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xvii) prepare plans or 15[ development schemes] for carrying out any of the above mentioned functions;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(xviii) any other function or functions which the Government may, from time to time, prescribe.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">16[ (2) The procedure prescribed by the Government from time to time for preparation and approval of development scheme shall apply in the matter of preparation and approval of development scheme of the Authority;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) [Omitted by section 6 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Powers regarding enforcement of certain rules, regulations and laws made by the Government</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The Authority shall, subject to permission and approval of the Government, have powers to enforce rules and regulations or any laws, either wholly or in part, pertaining to inland waterways and the control of traffic thereon.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">16. [Amendment and sanction of schemes.- Omitted by section 7 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Immunity of the Authority and its employees</p><p style="text-align: justify;">17.       (1) The Chairman, Members, officers and servants of the Authority shall, when acting or purporting to act in pursuance of any of the provisions of this Ordinance, be deemed to be public servants within the meaning of section 21 of the 17[ * * *] Penal Code.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No suit, prosecution or other legal proceedings shall lie against the Authority, the Chairman, Members or officers and servants of the Authority in respect of anything done or intended to be done, in good faith under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Submission of yearly reports and returns, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">18.       (1) The Authority shall submit to the Government, as soon as possible after the end of every financial year but before the last day of March next following, a report on the conduct of their affairs for that year.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Government may require the Authority to furnish:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) any return, statement, estimate, statistics or other information regarding any matter under the control of the Authority, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) a report on any such matter, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       a copy of any document in the charge of the Authority, and the Authority shall comply with every such requisition.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Authority Fund</p><p style="text-align: justify;">19. (1) There shall be a fund to be known as the “Authority Fund” vested in the Authority which shall be utilised by the Authority to meet charges in connection with their functions under this Ordinance including the payment of salaries and other remunerations to the Chairman and Members of the Authority and to their officers and servants.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Authority Fund shall consist of-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) grants made by the Government;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) loans obtained from the Government;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) tolls, taxes or fees in respect of the following items:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) inland waterways and the traffic thereon,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) shipping and navigation on tidal waters,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii) goods and passengers carried on inland waterways,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv) boats, launches and steamers on inland waters,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(v) tolls for maintenance of navigable waterways,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vi)       terminal taxes and other dues at inland ports,</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">And</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(vii)      fees for river conservancy works and pilotage services:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the following shall not form part of the Authority Fund:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) fees levied under Chapter II and III of the 18[ Inland Shipping Ordinance, 1976].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) taxes reserved for specified purposes.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">19[ (cc) The Government may empower the Authority to realise any or all of the tolls, taxes or fees specified in clause (c) of this sub-section.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        sale-proceeds of bonds issued under the authority of the Government;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        loans or grants obtained by the Authority with the special or general sanction of the Government;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         foreign aid and loans obtained from the Development Loan Fund or the International Bank of Reconstruction and Development or otherwise, with the sanction of, and on such terms and conditions as may be approved by the Government; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        all other sums received by the Authority.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The Government may levy tolls, taxes, fees or charges, in respect of all or any of the items, as specified in clause (c) of sub-section (2), at such rate and in such manner as are and/or as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">[]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">20[ 19A. [Power of the Government to levy tolls, taxes, fees or charges.- Omitted by section 4 of the East Pakistan Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1970 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. IX of 1970).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Recovery of tolls, taxes, fees, etc</p><p style="text-align: justify;">19B. Tolls, taxes, fees or charges levied under sub-section (3) of section 19 shall be recoverable as arrear of Land Revenue under the 21[ * * *] Public Demands Recovery Act, 1913.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Authority to be deemed to be a local authority</p><p style="text-align: justify;">20. The Authority shall be deemed to be a local authority under the Local Authorities Loans Act, 1914 for the purpose of borrowing money under the said Act, and the making and execution of any scheme under this Ordinance shall be deemed to be a work which such authority is legally authorised to carry out.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Limited liability</p><p style="text-align: justify;">21. The liability of the Government to the creditors of the Authority shall be limited to the extent of grants made by the Government and the loans raised by the Authority with the sanction of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Maintenance of accounts</p><p style="text-align: justify;">22. The Authority shall maintain complete and accurate books of accounts in such form as may be prescribed by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Budget</p><p style="text-align: justify;">22[ 23. The Authority shall, by such date in each year as may be prescribed, submit to the Government for approval a budget in the prescribed form for next financial year showing the estimated receipts and expenditure and the sums which are likely to be required from the Government during that financial year.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Audit</p><p style="text-align: justify;">23[ 24. (1) Without prejudice to the provisions of the Comptroller and Auditor General (Additional Functions) Act, 1974 (XXIV of 1974), the accounts of the Authority shall be audited by not less than two Auditors, being Chartered Accountants within the meaning of the Bangladesh Chartered Accountants Order, 1973 (P.O. No. 2 of 1973), who shall be appointed by the Authority, with the approval of the Government, on such remuneration to be paid by the Authority as the Government may fix.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The Authority shall carry out any directive issued by the Government for rectification of an audit objection.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">25. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of the Ordinance not otherwise specifically provided for.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the words “Bangladesh” and “Government” were substituted for the word “East Pakistan” and “Provincial Government” respectively by section 2 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “in East Pakistan” were omitted by section 3 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by Article 5 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Bangladesh Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by section 4 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 Sub-section (2) was substituted by section 2 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 Sub-sections (1) and (1A) were substituted for sub-section (1) by section 5 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 Sub-section (1A) was substituted by section 3 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">11 Section 14 was substituted by section 5 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">12 The words, figures and comma “section 59 of the Inland Shipping Ordinance, 1976” were substituted for the words, figures and comma “section 54A of the Inland Mechanically Propelled Vessels Act, 1917” by section 8 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">14 The words “maintain liaison with the Central Government and” were omitted by section 8 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">15 The words “development schemes” were substituted for the word “schemes” by section 6 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">17 The word “Pakistan” was omitted by section 9 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p Mechanically Propelled Vessels Act, 1917” by section 10 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">19 Clause (cc) was inserted by section 3 of the East Pakistan Inland Water Transport Authority (Second Amendment) Ordinance, 1959 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. XV of 1959)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">20 Sections 19A and 19B were inserted by section 4 of the East Pakistan Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1967 (East Pakistan Act No. X of 1967)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">21 The word “Bengal” was omitted by section 11 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Ordinance, 1977 (Ordinance No. LV of 1977)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">22 Section 23 was substituted by section 8 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">23 Section 24 was substituted by section 9 of the Inland Water Transport Authority (Amendment) Act, 1997 (Act No. IX of 1997)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
283	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">   THE POWER ALCOHOL ORDINANCE, 1959 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"><strong>THE POWER ALCOHOL ORDINANCE, 1959</strong></p><p align="center">(ORDINANCE NO. LIX OF 1959).</p><p align="right">[2nd December, 1959]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to make provision for certain matters connected with the development of the power alcohol industry.       1</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to make provision for certain matters connected with the development of the power alcohol industry under Federal control;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the seventh day of October 1958, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the President is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the Power Alcohol Ordinance, 1959.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 2[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) This section and section 2 shall come into force at once, and the rest of the Ordinance or such portion thereof shall come into force in such area and on such date as the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, specify in this behalf.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “molasses” means the heavy dark coloured residual syrup drained away in the final stage of the manufacture of sugar by vacuum pans in sugar factories either from sugarcane or by refining gur, when such a syrup has fermentable sugars (expressed as reducing sugars) but does not include the final residual left in the manufacture of sugar by the open pan process;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        “petrol” means dangerous petroleum as defined in clause (b) of section 2 of the Petroleum Act, 1934;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        “power alcohol” means ethyl alcohol containing not less than 99.5 per centum by volume of ethanol measured at sixty degrees Fahrenheit corresponding to 74.4 over proof strength.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Production of power alcohol</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) No person shall manufacture power alcohol from any substance other than molasses or such other substance as may be specified by the Government by notification in the official Gazette.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) If any dispute arises as to whether any substance is or is not molasses or such other substance as may be specified under sub-section (1), the decision of an officer authorised by the Government in this behalf regarding such dispute shall be final and shall not be called in question in any Court.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to regulate production and disposal of power alcohol</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. The Government may regulate the production and disposal of power alcohol by any distillery situated in any area in which this section is in force.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to direct use of power alcohol as motive power</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, direct that in such area as may be specified therein no petrol shall be sold or kept for sale except with an admixture of power alcohol.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The proportion of petrol and power alcohol in such mixture shall in any area and for any purpose be such as may from time to time be specified by the Government by notification in the official Gazette but such proportion of power alcohol in the case of mixture with petrol meant for use as motive power for any motor vehicle shall not be more than twenty-five per centum or less than five per centum by volume.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The power alcohol to be employed for such mixture shall be obtained from such distilleries as may from time to time be specified by the Government by notification in the official Gazette.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Penalty</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. Whoever contravenes any of the provisions of section 3 or section 5 or any order issued thereunder shall be punishable with imprisonment of either description for a term which may extend to six months, or with fine which may extend to one thousand rupees, or with both, and in the case of a continued contravention with a further fine which may extend to one hundred rupees for every day during which the contravention is continued after conviction therefore.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Delegation of powers</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, direct that any power conferred by this Ordinance shall, subject to such conditions, if any, as may be specified in the direction, be exercisable also by-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) such officer or authority subordinate to the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to make rules</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. (1) The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for the purpose of carrying into effect the provisions of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing powers, such rules may-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) provide for the licensing of the manufacture of power alcohol;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        prescribe the specifications and tests in respect of purity of power alcohol intended for admixture with petrol in order to ensure its suitability for use in motor vehicles;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        fix the price at which power alcohol may be sold for the purpose of admixture with petrol;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        provide for imposing and collecting a duty of excise on power alcohol intended for admixture with petrol;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        prescribe conditions in respect of the transport and storage of power alcohol intended for admixture with petrol and for the manner in which the admixture is to be effected;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         prescribe the submission by a manufacturer of power alcohol or importer or distributor of petrol of returns regarding the power alcohol and petrol manufactured, purchased, stored or sold, as the case may be;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        provide for denaturing of power alcohol at the distilleries;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h)        provide for any other matter which is to be or may be prescribed under this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Rules made under this Ordinance may provide that any contravention of any such rule shall render the offender liable on conviction to a fine not exceeding one thousand 4[ taka].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power of exemption</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette declare that any of the provisions of this Ordinance shall not apply to any case or class of cases.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">______________________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Central Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The word “ Bangladesh” was substituted for the word “Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 Clause (b) was omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “taka” was substituted for the word “rupees” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p>                       </div></div>
284	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">  THE PRIVATE FORESTS ORDINANCE, 1959   </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"> <strong>THE PRIVATE FORESTS ORDINANCE, 1959</strong></p><p align="center">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO.XXXIV OF 1959).</p><p align="right">[11th May, 1959]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to provide for the conservation of private forests and for the afforestation in certain cases of waste lands in Bangladesh.      1</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to provide for conservation of forests and for the afforestation of waste lands in Bangladesh where such forests or lands are not the property of the Government or where the Government have no proprietory right over such forests or lands;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND in pursuance of the Presidential Proclamation of the 7th day of October, 1958, and having received the previous instructions of the President, the Governor is pleased, in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p align="center" style="text-align: center;"><strong>CHAPTER I</strong></p><p align="center" style="text-align: center;"><strong>PRELIMINARY</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Short title, extent and commencement</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 2[ * * *] Private Forests Ordinance, 1959.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of Bangladesh.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) This section shall come into force at once and the remaining provisions of this Ordinance, in whole or in part, shall come into force in such areas and on such dates as the Government may, by notification, specify and for this purpose different dates may be specified for different provisions of this Ordinance and for different areas.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Definitions</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Ordinance, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(1)        “Appellate Committee” means a committee the procedure of which shall be as prescribed, appointed by the Government in respect of a notified area to hear appeal under this Ordinance consisting of three members of whom the Chairman shall be a Revenue Officer not below the rank of a Collector, one member shall be a Forest Officer not below the rank of a Deputy Conservator of Forests and the other member shall be an owner of a private forest who shall be selected in the prescribed manner from amongst the owners of private forests in such notified area;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2)        “cattle” includes elephants, camels, buffaloes, horses, mares, geldings, ponies, colts, fillies, mules, asses, pigs, rams, ewes, sheep, lambs, goats and kids;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) “conservation” used in reference to any forest land or waste land relates to such measures as are necessary in the opinion of the Regional Forest Officer for the prevention and remedying of deterioration of soil and its vegetative cover caused or likely to be caused through erosion, land-slide, flood, desiccation, burning, grazing, digging or removal of earth or through any other deteriorating agency and includes measures for improvement through protection, afforestation or any other means;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4)        “Controlled forest” means a private forest, not being vested forest in respect of which sections 2 to 63 of this Ordinance in whole or in part, have come into force;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3[ (5) “forest” includes any land recorded as forest in a record-of-rights prepared under Chapter IV of the State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950 (E.B. Act XXVIII of 1951) or such other land containing tree growth as may by notification be declared as forest by the Government;]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) “forest-offence” means an offence punishable under this Ordinance or under any rule made thereunder;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7)        “Forest Officer” means any person whom the Government or any officer empowered by the Government in this behalf, may appoint to carry out all or any of the purposes of this Ordinance or to do anything required by this Ordinance or any rule made thereunder to be done by a Forest Officer;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(8)        “forest-produce” includes-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the following whether found in, or brought from a forest or not, that is to say,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) timber, charcoal, caoutchouc, catechu, wood-oil, resin, natural varnish, bark, lac, mahua flowers, mahua seeds, kuth and myrabolans, and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        wild animals and skins, tusks, horns, bones, silks, cocoons, honey and wax, and all other parts or produce of animals, and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the following when found in, or brought from a forest, that is to say,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) trees and leaves, flowers and fruits, and all other parts, or produce not hereinbefore mentioned, of trees,</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) plants, not being trees (including grass, creepers, reeds and moss), and all parts or produce of such plants,</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii)       surface soil and rock (excluding salt rock and mineral rock), and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iv)       fish, tortoise, oysters, shells, sponge, conch, all crustacea and mollusca and all parts of produce of such fauna;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(9) “Forest Settlement Officer” means an officer who shall ordinarily be a Revenue Officer, appointed by the Government to perform the functions of a Forest Settlement Officer under this Ordinance, and includes a Board, the procedure of which shall be as prescribed, appointed by the Government to perform such functions, consisting of not more than three officers of whom at least two shall be Revenue Officers;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(10) “notification” means a notification published in the official Gazette;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(11) “notified area” means an area specified in a notification issued under sub-section (1) of section 3;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(12) “owner” includes any mortgagee in possession, lessee, common manager, receiver appointed by a competent Court and any person holding any property in trust and also includes a Court of Wards in respect of property under the superintendence or charge of such Court;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(13) “prescribed” means prescribed by rules made under this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(14) “private forest” means a forest which is not the property of the Government or over which the Government has no proprietory right;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(15)      “Regional Forest Officer” means a Forest Officer appointed as such by a notification for a notified area;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(16)      “river” includes any stream, canal, creek or other channel, natural or artificial;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(17) “timber” includes trees when they have fallen or have been felled, and all wood whether cut up or fashioned or hallowed out for any purpose or not;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(18) ‘tree' includes palms, bamboos, stumps, brushwood, canes, grasses, reeds, shrubs, herbs, etc.;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(19)      “vested forest” means a forest of which the control has been vested in a Regional Forest Officer by a notification under sub-section (2) of section 6 or under section 7 or under section 11 and includes any forest deemed to be or managed as, a vested forest under this Ordinance;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(20)      “waste-land” means any waste-land which is not the property of the Government or over which the Government has no proprietary right;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(21) “working plan” means a written plan prepared in the prescribed manner for the management and treatment of a forest or waste land; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(22)      “year” means a financial year.</p><p align="center">CHAPTER II</p><p align="center">CONSERVATION OF PRIVATE FORESTS AND AFFORESTATION OF WASTE LANDS</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Preparation of, and appeal and revision in respect of, working plans for private forest</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) (a) The Government may, by notification, direct that every owner of a private forest which is not a vested forest, but which is situated within such area as may be specified in the notification, shall prepare in the prescribed manner and submit within the period mentioned in the notification to the Regional Forest Officer a working plan for the conservation of such private forest.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) If any person fails to submit the statement mentioned in clause (a) of sub-section (1) within the specified time, he shall be punishable with fine which may extend to five hundred taka:</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that no prosecution shall be instituted under this sub-section unless the Regional Forest Officer has served in the prescribed manner a notice on such owner specifying his failure to carry out the above provision within 30 days from the date of service of such notice and unless such owner has failed to comply with such notice.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) On the expiry of the period mentioned in the notification under sub-section (1), the Regional Forest Officer shall, after considering each working plan submitted to him under that sub-section, and after consultation in the manner prescribed with the Conservator of Forests of the forest circle within which such forest is situated, by an order in writing, accept the working plan or modify it in such manner as he may consider necessary or substitute another working plan for it.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4[ (3a)] If any owner of such private forest does not submit a working plan within the period specified in the notification issued under sub-section (1), the Regional Forest Officer may, after consultation in the manner prescribed with the Conservator of Forests of the forest circle within which such forest is situated, prepare a working plan in respect of such forest.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5[ (3b) The cost of preparing the working plan under sub-section (3a) as estimated by the Regional Forest Officer in consultation with the Conservator of Forests of a circle within which such forest is situated, is recoverable from the owner of the private forest as forest revenue or as an arrear of forest revenue under the Public Demands Recovery Act, 1913.]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) When the Regional Forest Officer by an order in writing modifies any working plan under sub-section (2) or substitutes another working plan under that sub-section for the working plan submitted under sub-section (1), he shall cause a copy of such order to be served in the prescribed manner upon the owner of such private forest to which such working plan relates and such owner may, within sixty days of the date of service of such order, appeal against such order to the Appellate Committee and the Appellate Committee may thereupon, after giving such owner an opportunity of being heard, by an order in writing, either accept the working plan with or without modifications or reject it and the decision of the Appellate Committee on every such appeal shall, subject to the provisions of sub-section (5), be final.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The Board of Revenue may, on application by an owner of a private forest for revision of an order of the Appellate Committee passed in appeal under sub-section (4), and if such application is made within thirty days from the date of the order, call for the record of the appeal in which the order was passed and on receipt of such record, after giving such owner an opportunity of being heard, may, if it does not see fit to reject the application, direct the Appellate Committee by an order in writing to make such modifications in the working plan accepted by the said Committee under sub-section (4) as may be specified in such order in writing.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) The Board of Revenue shall, as soon as may be after an application for revision is disposed of under sub-section (5), communicate the order passed by it on such application to the Appellate Committee, and on receipt of such order the Appellate Committee shall, where the Board of Revenue has directed any modification to be made in such working plan, modify it accordingly.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Approved working plans</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) When the Appellate Committee accepts any working plan with or without modification under sub-section (4) of section 3, modifies any working plan under sub-section (6) of the said section, or the Regional Forest Officer accepts, modifies or substitutes any working plan under the said section or prepares any working plan under the said section, such Committee or officer shall, by an order in writing, approve such working plan or the working plan as so modified by the Committee or such officer, as the case may be, and every working plan so approved shall be deemed for the purposes of this Ordinance to be an approved working plan:</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Regional Forest Officer shall not so approve any working plan that he has modified or substituted by an order under sub-section (2) of section 3, if-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        an appeal against the order has been made to the Appellate Committee; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        where no such appeal has been made, the time within which such appeal may be made has not expired:</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided further that the Appellate Committee shall not so approve any working plan accepted by it with or without modification by an order under sub-section (4) of section 3 if,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) where an application for revision of the order has been made to the Board of Revenue, the order of the Board of Revenue on such application has not been received by such Committee; or</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) where no such application for revision has been made, the time within which such application may be made has not expired.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A copy of every approved working plan shall be sent in the prescribed manner by the Regional Forest Officer to the owner of the private forest to which it relates and the owner shall thereupon manage such forest in accordance with such plan and shall carry out all the terms and conditions thereof.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) At any time after five years from the date of approval of a working plan under sub-section (1), or with the previous sanction of the Government at any time within the said period of five years a Regional Forest Officer may, after consultation in the manner prescribed with the Conservator of Forests of the forest circle within which the forest to which such working plan relates is situated, by an order in writing, modify the approved working plan in such manner as he considers necessary and the provisions of sub-sections (4), (5) and (6) of section 3 and sub-sections (1) and (2) of this section shall apply to every plan so modified:</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that nothing in this section shall prevent the owner after the expiry of the said period of five years from applying in writing to the Regional Forest Officer for the modification of the working plan in such manner as may be specified in the application and if the Regional Forest Officer, after giving the owner an opportunity of being heard, does not see fit after such consultation as aforesaid so to modify the working plan, he shall record an order to that effect and the owner may, within thirty days from the date of such order, appeal against such order to the Appellate Committee and an application for revision shall also lie to the Board of Revenue from any order passed by the Appellate Committee on such appeal if presented within thirty days from the date of such order and the decision of the Appellate Committee on such appeal shall, subject to such revision by the Board of Revenue, be final.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Prohibition of leases of terms of existing leases of private
