286	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE PUBLIC INVESTMENTS (FINANCIAL SAFEGUARDS) ORDINANCE, 1960 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"><strong>THE PUBLIC INVESTMENTS (FINANCIAL SAFEGUARDS) ORDINANCE, 1960</strong></p><p align="center">(ORDINANCE NO. XLVI OF 1960)</p><p align="right">[2nd November, 1960]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance to provide for financial safeguards in respect of certain investments made out of public revenues.  1</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to provide for financial safeguards in respect of certain investments made out of public revenues;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Proclamation of the seventh day of October, 1958, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the President is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the Public Investments (Financial Safeguards) Ordinance, 1960.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. [Definition.- Omitted by section 3 of the Public Investments (Financial Safeguards) (Amendment) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. LVIII of 1976).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to Government to prescribe procedures, etc, in certain cases</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) Where any corporation, institution or undertaking, whether incorporated in pursuance of a 2[ Bangladesh law] or not so incorporated, has been established by Government with the aid of public revenues, the Government shall, notwithstanding anything in any law, or in any instrument, deed or other document relating to such corporation, institution or undertaking, have power-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        to prescribe financial procedures, including procedures for internal financial control, in respect of matters relating</p><p style="text-align: justify;">to the receipt and expenditure of moneys and sanctions thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) to give general or special financial directions to such corporations, institutions and undertakings; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        to depute such of its officer or officers to scrutinise their financial procedures and transactions as it may think necessary.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Where any procedure is prescribed under clause (a) of sub-section (1), or any financial direction is given, or officer deputed, under clause (b) or clause (c) thereof, it shall be the duty of the Corporation, institution or undertaking concerned to comply with the procedure or direction, or, as the case may be, to receive the officer and afford him every convenient means of fulfilling the purpose of his deputation.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to Government to give directions in certain other cases</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. Where any corporation has been established otherwise than by Government, but Government, or any such corporation, institution or undertaking as is referred to in section 3, has provided a portion of the capital or funds thereof, and is thereby entitled to appoint one or more Directors, the Government may, notwithstanding anything in the 3[ Companies Act, 1994 (Act 18 of 1994)], or in any other law, or in any instrument, deed or other document relating thereto, give the director or directors so appointed such general or special financial directions as it may think necessary, and it shall be the duty of every such director to comply with the directions so given.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to call for documents, etc</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. The Government may, in order to ensure proper compliance with the provisions of this Ordinance, call for any information, including any book, account, record or other document, from any such corporation, institution or undertaking as is referred to in section 3, or from any such director as is referred to in section 4.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Penalties</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. Whoever fails to discharge any duty imposed by or under this Ordinance, or to comply with any direction given or any rule or order made or issued thereunder, shall be punishable with simple imprisonment for a term which may extend to three months, or with fine which may extend to 4[ Taka fifty thousand] , or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Offences by Corporations, etc</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. If an offence punishable under this Ordinance is committed by a Corporation, institution or undertaking, every director, manager, secretary, agent or other officer or person concerned with the management thereof, shall, unless he proves that the offence was committed without his knowledge or consent, or that he exercised due diligence to prevent its commission, be deemed to be guilty of such offence.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>False information, etc</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. Any person who,</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        when required under this Ordinance to furnish any information, furnishes any information which is false in any material particular and which he knows or has reasonable cause to believe to be false, or does not believe to be true, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        knowingly makes any false statement in any book, account, record or other document which he is required under this Ordinance to furnish,</p><p style="text-align: justify;">shall be punishable with the same punishment as is provided in section 6.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Cognizance of offence</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. No Court inferior to that of a Magistrate of the First Class shall take cognizance of any offence punishable under this Ordinance, and cognizance shall not be so taken save on a complaint made in writing by or under the authority of the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to make rules</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">______________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “appropriate Government” by section 2 of the Public Investments (Financial Safeguards) (Amendment) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. LVIII of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “Bangladesh law” were substituted for the words “Central or Provincial law” by section 4 of the Public Investments (Financial Safeguards) (Amendment) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. LVIII of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words, comma, figures and brackets “Companies Act, 1994 (Act 18 of 1994)” were substituted for the words, comma, brackets and figure “Companies Act, 1913 (VII of 1913)” by section 3 of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision and Declaration) (Third Amendment) Act, 2001 (Act No. XLVIII of 2001)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The words “Taka fifty thousand” were substituted for the words “ten thousand rupees” by section 5 of the Public Investments (Financial Safeguards) (Amendment) Ordinance, 1976 (Ordinance No. LVIII of 1976)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p>                       </div></div>
287	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE RENT RECEIPT ORDINANCE, 1959 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"><strong>THE RENT RECEIPT ORDINANCE, 1959</strong></p><p align="center">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. LVII OF 1959)</p><p align="right">[15th August, 1959]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">An Ordinance  to make provision for prevention of issue, possession and use of ante-dated rent-receipt by any person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS it is expedient to make provision for prevention of issue, possession and use of ante-dated rent-receipt by any person;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Presidential Proclamation of the seventh day of October, 1958, and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor of East Pakistan is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the 1[ * * *] Rent-receipt Ordinance, 1959.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 2[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Prohibition of issue, possession and use of ante-dated rent-receipt</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. Whoever issues any ante-dated rent-receipt or amalnama or has in his possession any ante-dated rent-receipt or amalnama, knowing or having reason to believe the same to be ante-dated, or uses the same as genuine, shall be punished with imprisonment for a term which may extend to five years, or with fine, or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">__________________________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The word “ Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p>                       </div></div>
288	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE SAIRAT MAHALS (MANAGEMENT) ORDINANCE, 1959 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p align="center"><strong>THE SAIRAT MAHALS (MANAGEMENT) ORDINANCE, 1959</strong></p><p align="center">(EAST PAKISTAN ORDINANCE NO. VI OF 1959)</p><p align="right">[12th January, 1959]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 WHEREAS shares in some hats, bazars, fisheries and ferries, have vested in the Government as a result of acquisition of interests under provisions of the 2[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, or otherwise;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS joint ownership of such hats, bazars, fisheries and ferries by the Government along with others has often led and is likely to lead to unnecessary litigation, double realisation of tolls, breach of the peace and harassment to the public in other ways;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS with a view to removing such difficulties, it is necessary to make provisions for the management and control by the Government of the shares of such hats, bazars, fisheries and ferries held by others;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">NOW, THEREFORE, in pursuance of the Presidential Proclamation of the 7th day of October, 1958 and in exercise of all powers enabling him in that behalf, the Governor is pleased to make and promulgate the following Ordinance, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Ordinance may be called the Sairat Mahals (Management) Ordinance, 1959.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 3[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Assumption of possessions management and control by the Government</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. (1) Where any share of any hat, bazar, fishery or ferry has vested in the Government as a result of acquisition under the 4[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, or otherwise, the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, assume the right of possession, management and control of the remaining share or shares of such hat, bazar, fishery or ferry.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Immediately upon the publication of a notification under sub-section (1), the right of possession, management and control of such share or shares in the hat, bazar, fishery or ferry shall pass on to the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Where the right of possession, management and control of any share in any hat, bazar, fishery or ferry has passed on to the Government under sub-section (2), the owner of such share shall, from the date of such passing on till the date of vesting of such share in the Government as a result of acquisition under the provisions of the 5[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, or otherwise, receive from the Government in respect of such share as compensation for use and occupation for each year or part of a year an amount which will bear such proportion to the net income realised by the Government for the entire property for that year or part of a year as such share bears to the whole property.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) In calculating the net income referred to in sub-section (3) for any such property for any year or part of a year, there shall be deducted from the gross proceeds received by the Government from such property on account of such year or part of a year,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) any rent payable on account of such year or part of a year for such property to any superior landlord whose interests have not been acquired;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        all expenses incurred for khas management of the property where the Government manages the property in khas;</p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c)        in case the property is let out by the Government, the cost of advertisement and holding the sale, any refund or abatement that may have to be made to the lessee under the terms of the lease and other expenses, if any, incurred by the Government in connection with the management of such property.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Bar to the jurisdiction of Courts</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. No Court shall entertain any suit or proceeding to restrain the Government from assuming the right of possession, management and control of any share in any hat, bazar, fishery or ferry in pursuance of any notification issued under sub-section (1) of section 2.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Relinquishment of possession, management, etc</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. The Government may, at any time, by notification in the official Gazette, relinquish possession, management and control of a share or shares of which possession, management and control have been assumed under section 2 and upon publication of such notification, the right of possession, management and control shall pass back to the previous owners.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"><b>Power to make rules</b></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. The Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, make rules for the purpose of carrying into effect the provisions of this Ordinance.</p><p style="text-align: justify;">__________________________________________________________</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Ordinance, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The word “ Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “ East Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p>                       </div></div>
289	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE STATE ACQUISITION (AD-INTERIM PAYMENT) ACT, 1957 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE STATE ACQUISITION (AD-INTERIM PAYMENT) ACT, 1957 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ACT NO. XXXIII OF 1957).[26th October, 1957]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">An  Act to make provisions for more expeditious ad-interim payment.     1</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS under sub-section (1) of section 6 of the 2[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, a rent-receiver whose rent-receiving interests not held under wakf, wakf-al-aulad, debutter or any other trust are acquired under sub-section (1) of section 3 of that Act is, with effect from the date of acquisition, entitled to receive annually in cash in respect of such interests an ad-interim payment at the rate of one-third of the net income on account of the demands of rent and cesses for any period after the date of acquisition collected by the Government for such interests in the year to which such payment relates;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS in the cases of such rent-receiving interests acquired after the 1st April, 1956, under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the said Act, it will take much time to collect necessary details and start and maintain separate accounts of collections of rents and cesses made by the Government in respect of such rent-receiving interests held by each rent-receiver for complying with the provisions of sub-section (1) of section 6 of the said Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS the making of ad-interim payments in such cases according to the provision of sub-section (1) of section 6 of the said Act will in the aforesaid circumstances, be much delayed and will consequently cause much hardship to the rent-receivers concerned;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS in order to avoid such hardship, it is considered expedient to make provisions for more expeditious ad-interim payments in such cases on a simpler basis;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Short title, extent and commencement</p><p style="text-align: justify;">1. (1) This Act may be called the 3[ * * *] State Acquisition (Ad-interim Payment) Act, 1957.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 4[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Definitions</p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant to the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(1)        “prescribed” means prescribed by rules made under this Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2)        “Revenue-officer” includes any officer whom the Government may appoint to discharge all or any of the functions of a Revenue-officer under this Act or any rules made thereunder; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) all other words and expressions used in this Act shall have the same meanings as in the 5[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Ad-interim payment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in sub-sections (1), (3) and (4) of section 6 of the 6[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950 (hereinafter referred to as the said Act), a rent-receiver, whose interests in any estate, taluk, tenure, holding or tenancy or part thereof, not held under wakf, wakf-al-aulad, debutter or any other trust, have been acquired under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the said Act after the 1st day of April, 1956, shall, with effect from the date of such acquisition, be entitled to receive annually, in cash, in respect of such interests, at such time and in such manner as may be prescribed, an ad-interim payment at the rate of one-sixth of the net income calculated according to the provisions in sub-section (2).</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) For the purposes of sub-section (1), the net income of a rent-receiver from any estate, taluk, tenure, holding or tenancy or part thereof shall be calculated by deducting from the gross assets, consisting of the aggregate of the rents and cesses which were payable to such rent-receiver by his immediately subordinate tenants in such estate, taluk, tenure, holding, tenancy or part thereof for the agricultural year immediately preceding the date of acquisition, the following, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the sums which were or are calculated as payable by such rent-receiver for such year as land revenue or rent and cesses to the Government or to his immediate landlord, as the case may be, in respect of such estate, taluk, tenure, holding, tenancy or part thereof;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) the sums which were or are calculated as payable by such rent-receiver in respect of such assets for such year as taxes under the Bengal Agricultural Income-tax Act, 1944 and the 7[ Income-tax Ordinance, 1984 (XXXVI of 1984)];</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the average annual expenditure, if any, incurred by such rent-receiver on account of maintenance of any irrigation or protective works in such estate, taluk, tenure, holding, tenancy, or part thereof; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        collection charges not exceeding twenty per centum of the gross assets.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) In calculating the amounts of deduction under sub-section (2), the Revenue-officer shall be guided by such rules as may be made in this behalf by the Government.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Service of notice to furnish statements</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. (1) For the purpose of calculating the net income under section 3, the Revenue-officer shall publish a proclamation in the prescribed manner in every village requiring the rent-receivers concerned to furnish, within sixty days from the date of publication of the proclamation or within such further time as may be allowed by the Revenue-officer on application, statements in the prescribed forms showing therein their gross assets and deductible amounts as referred to in sub-section (2) of section 3 and such other particulars as may be prescribed:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that the Government may, at any time, by notification in the official Gazette, allow such of the rent-receivers, as have not already furnished such statements in pursuance of the said Proclamation, a second opportunity to furnish the same to the Revenue-Officer within such period as may be specified in the notification.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The net income shall be calculated by the Revenue-officer after considering the returns furnished under sub-section (1) and making such enquiry as he thinks fit.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) The submission of the statements required under sub-section (1) shall be the condition precedent to the making of ad-interim payments under section 3.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Appeal</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. Any person aggrieved by an order of the Revenue-officer determining the amount of any ad-interim payment under section 3 may, within a prescribed period and in the prescribed manner, present an appeal in writing to a prescribed superior Revenue Authority, and the decision of such Authority and also, subject only to such decision an order of the Revenue-officer passed under that section shall be final.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Exemption of ad-interim payment from attachment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. Notwithstanding anything contained in the Code of Civil Procedure, 1908, and the 8[ * * *] Public Demands Recovery Act, 1913, any amount payable to a rent-receiver under section 3 shall not be liable to attachment in execution of any decree or order of a Civil Court or of a certificate signed under the 9[ * * *] Public Demands Recovery Act, 1913, other than a decree or certificate for the recovery of arrears of revenue, rent or cesses due in respect of the interests to which such payment relates.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Ceasing of ad-interim payments and adjustment thereof</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. With effect from the 1st day of the agricultural year next following the date of publication in the official Gazette of a notification under sub-section (2) of section 43 of the said Act, declaring that a Compensation Assessment-roll has been finally published, the ad-interim payment under section 3 in respect of the interest for which compensation has been assessed in such roll shall cease; and the total amount of ad-interim payments made under section 3 in respect of any such interests, less an amount calculated at the rate of three per centum per annum on the amount of compensation assessed for such interests in such roll from the date of acquisition of such interests under sub-section (1) of section 3 of the said Act till the last day of the agricultural year in which such notification is so published, shall be deducted from the amount of such compensation before proceeding to make payment of such compensation under sub-section (1) of section 58 of the said Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[Omitted]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. [Option.- Omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10[Repealed]</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10. [Repeal and saving.- Repealed by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Repealing and Amending Ordinance, 1966 (East Pakistan Ordinance No. XIII of 1966).]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The words, comma, figures and brackets “Income-tax Ordinance 1984 (XXXVI of 1984)” were substituted for the words, comma, figures and brackets “Income-tax Act, 1922 (XI of 1922)” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 The word “Bengal” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The word “Bengal” was omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Source : Ministry of Law, Justice and Parliamentary Affairs</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p> </div></div>
290	<h2 class="blog_entry-title">THE STATE ACQUISITION (BONDS) ACT, 1957 </h2>
<div class="entry-content"><div class="entry-content"><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong>THE STATE ACQUISITION (BONDS) ACT, 1957 </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(EAST PAKISTAN ACT NO. XXXVIII OF 1957).[23rd November, 1957]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 An Act to make certain provisions in connection with the issue and management of bonds mentioned in sub-section (2) of section 58 of the 2[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">WHEREAS sub-section (2) of section 58 of the 3[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950, provides for payment of compensation either in cash or in bonds or partly in cash and partly in bonds;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4[ * * *]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">AND WHEREAS it is expedient to make certain provisions in connection with the issue and management of such bonds and payment of instalments thereunder and for other matters incidental thereto;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">It is hereby enacted as follows:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Short title, extent and commencement </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1.         (1) This Act may be called the 5[ * * *] State Acquisition (Bonds) Act, 1957.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) It extends to the whole of 6[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) It shall come into force at once.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"><strong> Definitions </strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2. In this Act, unless there is anything repugnant in the subject or context,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        “the Act” means the 7[ * * *] State Acquisition and Tenancy Act, 1950;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8[ (b) “Bank” means the Bangladesh Bank established under the Bangladesh Bank Order, 1972 (P. O. No. 127 of 1972);]</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) “Bond” means a Bond referred to in sub-section (2) of section 58 of the Act;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d)        “management” of bonds includes subdivision, consolidation and renewal of bonds and issue of duplicate bonds;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e)        “prescribed” means prescribed by rules made by the Government under this Act; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f)         “Public Debt Office” means the Public Debt Office of the 9[ Bangladesh Bank].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Form and denominations of Bonds and issue and management thereof</p><p style="text-align: justify;">3. The work of issue and management of Bonds and payment of instalments thereunder shall be done by the Bank in accordance with such rules, and the form and denominations of the Bonds shall be such, as may be prescribed.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Discharge of Government from liabilities</p><p style="text-align: justify;">4. The Government shall be discharged from all liabilities in respect of a Bond when all the instalments due thereon have been paid or when a duplicate, new or renewed Bond has been issued in its place.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Holding of Bonds in name of public office</p><p style="text-align: justify;">5. (1) In the case of any public office to which the Government may, by notification in the official Gazette, declare this sub-section to apply, a Bond may be held in the name of the office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) When a Bond is so held, it shall be deemed to be transferred without any or further transfer deed from each holder of the office to the succeeding holder of the office on and from the date on which the latter takes charge of the office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) This section applies as well to an office of which there are two or more joint holders as to an office of which there is a single holder.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Holding of Bonds as trustee or by an Office other than public office</p><p style="text-align: justify;">6. (1) No notice of any trust in respect of any Bond shall be receivable by the Government, nor shall the Government be bound by any such notice even though expressly given, nor shall the Government be regarded as trustee in respect of any Bond.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) Without prejudice to the provisions of sub-section (1), the Bank may, as an act of grace and without any liability to the Bank or to the Government, record in its books such directions by the holder of a Bond for the payment of instalments due on a Bond or such other matters relating to a Bond, as the Bank thinks fit.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) Bonds may be held by a holder of an office, other than a public office,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a)        in his personal name, described in the books of the Public Debt Office and in the Bond as a trustee, whether as a trustee of the trust specified in his application or as a trustee without any such qualification, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        by the name of his office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) On an application made in writing to the Public Debt Office, in the form required by that Office, by the person in whose name a Bond stands, and on surrender of the Bond, the Public Debt Office may-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) make an entry in their books describing him as a trustee of a specified trust or as a trustee without specification</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">of any trust and issue a Bond in his name described as trustee with or without the specification of the trust, as the case may be, or</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        issue a Bond to him by the name of his office and make entry in its books describing him as the holder of the Bond by the name of his office, according to the applicant's request:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) the request is in conformity with the provisions of sub-section (3); and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii)        the necessary evidence required by the Public Debt Office in terms of sub-section (9) has been furnished.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) The Bond under sub-section (3) may be held by the holder of the office either alone or jointly with a person or persons holding an office, other than a public office, or another person or an official authorised to hold the Bond by the name of his office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) When a Bond is held by a person in the name of his office, any document relating to the Bond may be executed by the person for the time being holding the office by the name in which the Bond is held as if his personal name were so stated.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7) Where any transfer deed, power of attorney or other document purporting to be executed by a Bond-holder described in the books of the Public Debt Office as trustee or as a holder of an office is produced to the Public Debt Office, the Public Debt Office shall not be concerned to inquire whether the executant is entitled under the terms of any trust or document to give any such power or to execute such deed or other document and may act on the transfer deed, power of attorney or document in the same manner as though the executant is a Bond-holder and whether the Bond-holder is or is not described in the transfer deed, power of attorney or document as a trustee or as a holder of an office and whether he does or does not purport to execute the transfer deed, power of attorney or document in his capacity as a trustee or as a holder of the office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(8) Nothing in this Act shall, as between any trustees and office-holders, or as between any trustees or office-holders and the beneficiaries, under a trust or any document, be deemed to authorise the trustees or office-holders to act otherwise than in accordance with the provisions of law applicable to trust, the terms of the instrument constituting the trust, or the rules governing the association, of which the Bond-holder is a holder of an office; and neither the Government nor any person holding or acquiring any interest in any Bond shall, by reason only of any entry in any register maintained by or on behalf of the Government or the Bank in relation to any Bond or of anything in any document relating to Bond, be affected with notice of any trust or of the fiduciary character of any holder of any Bond or of any fiduciary obligation attaching to the holding of any Bond.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(9) Before acting on any application made, or on any document purporting to be executed in pursuance of this section by a person as being the holder of any office, the Public Debt Office may require the production of evidence that such person is the holder for the time being of that Office.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Recognition of title to Bonds</p><p style="text-align: justify;">7. The executors or administrators of a deceased sole holder of a Bond and the holder of a succession certificate issued under Part X of the Succession Act, 1925, shall be the only persons who may be recognised by the Bank as having any title to the Bond:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that nothing in this section shall bar the recognition by the Bank of the manager or the sole surviving male member of a Hindu undivided family governed by the Mitakshara Law as having a title to a Bond, when the Bond appears to the Bank to stand in the name of a deceased member of the family and an application is made by such manager or sole surviving member for recognition of his title and is supported by a certificate issued by the District Magistrate after such inquiry as may in his opinion be necessary to the effect that the deceased belonged to a Hindu undivided family governed by the Mitakshara Law, that the Bond formed part of the joint property of the family, and that the applicant is the managing or sole surviving male member of the family.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Rights of survivors of joint holders and summary procedure in certain cases</p><p style="text-align: justify;">8. (1) Notwithstanding anything contained in section 45 of the Contract Act, 1872,-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) when a Bond is held by two or more persons jointly and either or any of them dies, the title to the Bond shall vest in the survivor or survivors of those persons; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        when a Bond is payable to two or more persons severally and either or any of them dies, the Bond shall be payable to the survivor or survivors of those persons or to the representatives of the deceased or to any of them:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that nothing contained in this section shall affect any claim which any representative of a deceased person may have against the survivor or survivors under or in respect of any Bond to which this section applies.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) (i) Notwithstanding anything contained in section 7, if, within six months of the death of a person who was the holder of a Bond or Bonds the face-value of which does not in the aggregate exceed five thousand rupees, probate of his Will or letters of administration of his estate or a succession certificate issued under Part X of the Succession Act, 1925, is not produced to the Bank, or proof to the satisfaction of the Bank that proceedings have been instituted to obtain one of these is not furnished, the Bank may determine who is the person entitled to the Bond or Bonds or to administer the estate of the deceased and may make an order vesting the Bond or Bonds in the person so determined.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) When a Bond or Bonds belong to a minor or a person who is insane and incapable of managing his affairs and the face-value of the Bond or Bonds does not in the aggregate exceed five thousand rupees, the Bank may make such order as it thinks fit for the vesting of such Bond or Bonds in such person as it considers represents the minor or insane person.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Determination of person entitled to a Bond</p><p style="text-align: justify;">9. (1) If the Bank is of opinion that a doubt exists as to the title to a Bond or in cases of the Bonds to which clauses (i) or (ii) of sub-section (2) of section 8 apply, the Bank may determine the person in the manner hereunder as being entitled in its opinion to the Bond and payment of all accrued and accruing instalments and may by its order vest title in such person accordingly.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) The person claiming to be entitled to a Bond or to payment of accrued and accruing instalments due thereon shall apply to the Bank and adduce documentary evidence in support of his claim.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) On receipt of the application by the Bank, the Bank, if it contemplates making a vesting order, may, if it considers proper, request a District Magistrate to record or to have recorded the whole or any part of such evidence as any person whose evidence the Bank requires may produce or direct one of its officers to record such evidence or may receive evidence upon affidavit. Nothing herein shall preclude the Bank from determining title without enquiry in the manner laid down in this sub-section.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(4) The Bank shall thereafter give notice in writing to each claimant of whom it has knowledge stating the names of all other claimants and the time when and the officer of the Bank by whom the determination of title will be made.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(5) On the date and at the time fixed in the notice, the officer shall-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) examine the evidence adduced by the parties;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(ii) hear the parties affected and record such evidence as they adduce:</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Provided that no further evidence shall be recorded or entertained in cases where the District Magistrate has been requested to record or to have evidence recorded, or the Bank has directed one of its officers to record the evidence; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(iii) determine the issue as to who is entitled to the Bond.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(6) After determination of the issue by the officer, the Bank shall give to each claimant notice in writing of the determination so made.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(7) The notices under sub-sections (4) and (6) shall be published in three successive issues of the 10[ * * *] official Gazette as soon as possible after the date on which they are respectively issued.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(8) The Bank may require the person considered by the Bank as being entitled to the Bond or to instalments due thereon to execute a security bond in the prescribed form with one or more sureties or to furnish security not exceeding twice the value of the subject-matter of the order, to be held at the disposal of the Bank, to pay to the Bank or to any person, to whom the Bank may assign the security bond or the security in furtherance of sub-section (2) of section 13 of this Act, the amount thereof.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(9) On the expiry of six months from the publication under sub-section (7) of the notice issued under sub-section (6), the Bank may make an order vesting the Bond and any instalments due thereon in the person found by the Bank to be entitled thereto.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(10) Notwithstanding anything contained in this section, the Bank may vest-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) title limited to drawal of instalments in guardian of a minor or a manager of the property of an insane person, and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b) full title in the minor or the insane person to take effect on the minor attaining the age of majority or on the insane person becoming sane.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Determination of rights</p><p style="text-align: justify;">10.       The rights of all persons in relation to the Bonds shall be determined in connection with all such questions as are dealt with by this Act by the law and in the Courts of 11[ Bangladesh].</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Recording of evidence</p><p style="text-align: justify;">11.       (1) For the purpose of making any order which it is empowered to make under this Act, the Bank may request a District Magistrate to record or to have recorded the whole or any part of such evidence as any person whose evidence the Bank requires may produce. The District Magistrate so requested may himself record or may direct any Magistrate subordinate to him to record the evidence and shall forward a copy thereof to the Bank.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) For the purpose of making a vesting order under this Act, the Bank may direct one of its officers to record the evidence of any person whose evidence the Bank requires or may receive evidence upon affidavit.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(3) A Magistrate or an officer of the Bank acting in pursuance of this Act may administer an oath to any witness examined by him.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Suspension of payment and postponement of order and registration</p><p style="text-align: justify;">12.       Where the Bank contemplates making an order under this Act to vest a Bond in any person, the Bank may suspend payment of instalments due on the Bond or postpone the renewal of the Bond or the issue of any duplicate Bond or of any new Bond or Bonds in lieu thereof or the registration of any transfer of the Bond, until the vesting order has been made.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Bank may require security</p><p style="text-align: justify;">13.       (1) Before making any order which it is empowered to make under this Act, the Bank may require the person in whose favour the order is to be made to execute a security bond with one or more sureties in the prescribed form or to furnish security not exceeding twice the value of the subject-matter of the order, to be held at the disposal of the Bank, to pay to the Bank or any person, to whom the Bank may assign the security bond or the security in furtherance of sub-section (2), the amount thereof.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) A Court before which a claim in respect of the subject-matter of any such order is established may order the security bond or the security to be assigned to the successful claimant who shall thereupon be entitled to enforce the security bond or realise the security to the extent of such claim.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Effect of recognition by the Bank of a person as the holder of a Bond</p><p style="text-align: justify;">14.       No recognition by the Bank of a person as the holder of a Bond and no order made by the Bank under this Act shall be called in question by any Court so far as such recognition or order affect the relation of the Government or the Bank with the person recognised by the Bank as the holder of a Bond or with any person claiming an interest in such bond; and any such recognition by the Bank of any person or any order by the Bank vesting a Bond in any person shall operate to confer on that person a title to the bond subject only to a personal liability to the rightful owner of the Bond for money had and received on his account.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Cancellation of proceedings</p><p style="text-align: justify;">15.       Where the Bank contemplates making an order under this Act vesting a Bond in any person, the Bank may, at any time before the order is made, cancel any proceedings already taken for that purpose and may, on such cancellation, proceed anew to the making of such order.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Bar to claiming of interest on instalment</p><p style="text-align: justify;">16.       No person shall be entitled to claim interest on the instalment due on a Bond in respect of any period which has elapsed after the earliest date on which demand could have been made for the payment of the instalment.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Penalty for false statement</p><p style="text-align: justify;">17. (1) If any person, for the purpose of obtaining for himself or for any other person any title to a Bond, makes to any authority under this Act, in any application or in the course of any enquiry, any statement which is false and which he either knows to be false or does not believe to be true, he shall be punishable with imprisonment for a term which may extend to six months, or with fine, or with both.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) No Court shall take cognizance of any offence under sub-section (1) except on the complaint of the Bank.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">Power to make rules</p><p style="text-align: justify;">18.       (1) The Government may make rules for carrying out the purposes of this Act.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(2) In particular and without prejudice to the generality of the foregoing power, such rules may provide for all or any of the following matters, namely:-</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(a) the authority which can make requisition for issue of Bonds and the procedure and form for making such requisition;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(b)        the form and denomination of Bonds and payment of instalments thereunder;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(c) the manner of issue, enfacement and delivery of Bonds;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(d) the issue of duplicate Bonds and subdivision, consolidation and renewal thereof;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(e) the form of security bond under sub-section (8) of section 9 and sub-section (1) of section 13;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(f) the circumstances requiring renewal of Bonds;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(g)        the manner of application for information or inspection and the circumstances under which information may be supplied or inspection may be allowed;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(h) the fees for renewal, consolidation or subdivision of Bonds and issue of duplicate Bonds and for information and inspection and in other matters;</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(i) the powers of the Bank in procedural matters; and</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">(j) the manner of service of notices.</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">1 Throughout this Act, the word “Government” was substituted for the words “Provincial Government” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">2 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">3 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">4 Second paragraph to the preamble was omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">5 The words “East Pakistan” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">6 The word “Bangladesh” was substituted for the words “East Pakistan” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">7 The words “East Bengal” were omitted by Article 6 of the Bangladesh (Adaptation of Existing Laws) Order, 1972 (President's Order No. 48 of 1972)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">8 Clause (b) was substituted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">9 The words “Bangladesh Bank” were substituted for the words “State Bank of Pakistan at Dacca” by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p style="text-align: justify;">10 The words “Gazette of Pakistan and the local” were omitted by section 3 and the Second Schedule of the Bangladesh Laws (Revision And Declaration) Act, 1973 (Act No. VIII of 1973)</p><p style="text-align: justify;"></p><p
